inspiciendum et ex ammandu antequam fue rat libere comuicata qui post ispectione eiusdem perdies aliquot retradens ipsum librum memorato eiusde libri proprie vocis oraculo singulis comedauit et approbauit nec et auctoritate sua metropolitica vt pote catholicum publice cominicandum decreuit et mandauit ad fidelium e dificacionem et hereticoru siue lollardorum confutacionem qvecun que scripta companye falle doune wyth lucyfer hadden grete compsyon soo longe meschyef man made restorynge prayden ofte restoryng specialli wyth instaunce whan tyme grace come tyme may deuoutly ymagyne blessyd companye aungels gadred gydre wyth one wyll souereyne deuocyon fellen doune prostrate fore tronen almyghty god kynge heuen gabriel whome seynte bernard saith made speciall reuelacion crystes incarnacon owne name sayd thys maner p almyghty lord hit lyked youre hyghe mageste endles goodnes make nouyt noble resonable creature man oure comforte oure goodnes hym shold made restoryng oure fals companye lucifer hys felawes felle doune fro v apostasye soo sholde dwelle thys blessyd place wyth v louynge worshyppyng yow wythouten ende loo go od lord thei perysshen none saued many thousand yere passed sene none hem oure enemyes hauen vyctorye hem oure partye restored pryson helle contynuelly fylled wher lord borne grete meschyef though doune ryytwysnes neuertheles lord tyme mercy haue mynde ye made hem youre owne lykenes though fornfaders folyly wrechydly breken youre maudement neuertheles youre mercy aboue al thynge wherfore eyen ben set vpon seruautes lordes handes tyll ye haue mercy helpe hem wyth spedeful heleful remedy seqiut de cotencoe iter miam veritatem phere wyth beganne maner altercacion disputacion bytuene foure kynges deughters saye marcy sothfastnes pee ryght wysnesse whiche foure mercy pee accordyng aungels prayer sayde fauourable mannes restorynge two systers sothbe r de fastnes right wysnes ageyne sayden p saynte bernarde deuout ditacion maketh herof processe faire longe take therof shortly purpos tyme sowhat maner wordes may ymagyne thynke th fyrst mercy pee knelyng fore fader kyng heuen phetes wordes dauid said thus lord shalt thou cast anunquid num p ci de u way fro withoute ende hast thou foryete mercy oft reherceden said lord lete clepe forth two systers whyche ye sene redy ayenste lete v see also wol saye weremiser cor n cleped comen al gyder mercy began said wyse fader mercy youre wyl euer withouten ende moge douyters systers yeue prerogatyue aboue al werkes shold specially regne wyth heuen also erthe shold replenyshed wyth soo moche vertu wold truly besely aske helpe ony meschyef nede shold wythout fayl finde socour helpe thoruy meditacon lo dere fader worthi partie erthe noble creature man hys grete wretchydnesse myschyef longe made man grete worthynes ye wedded codycyon tyme breke heste al come hym shold lese blessyd lyf dapned done deth wherfore forsoke betoke hym enmy myn fader lesyng witnes syster riytwysnes perysshe lese name haue deth hath deseruyd tha spake riytwysjus jus e ne ryytwis lord thou hast made gouernour thi dome lastyng wythoute ende sister trouth techer thy lawe al thouy sister mercy styred pyte good zele mannes sauacyon neuertheles wolde saue hym hath gretely forfetyd ageinst yow v alsoca withouten dewe satisfaccion wolde destroye v hir susteren say trouthe ryghtwysnes fordo namepa fourth syster came forth saye pee irite sovirly blamyng hir susters contrarious wordes stryt said hem thus knowe ye wel sister thatin pace actu ocu fader hath ordeyned made place may abyde ne dwelle stryf dissecion semely fully ageynst kynde amoges vertues wherfor ye cease stryf acorded must forsake yow fader also lo agrete cotrauersy bytwene se four douyters lorde grete reason sene mannes sauacion mercy sothfastnes pee ryytwysnes myght fully kepte accorded badpater udicuim de di fader heuen moche comytted ye uen dome dere sone souerayne wysedome kyng euerlastyng one godhede four douyters shold go hym termyne question yeue dome ther kynge souerayne wysedome wrote se te e dome thys maner toke hys chauceler reson rede name sayenge wordes doughter sothfastnes saith peryssheth leseth hyr name man haue deth hath deserued hyr acordeth hir lister riytwysnes syde mercy sayth perissheth leseth hir name man haue mercy saued hir accordeth fourth sister pee wherfor accorde gyder fynal dome mater douyter al grace hade wythoute trauayle nay telle wete grace yefte ne vertue god withoute grete trauaylle contynuel prayer ardent desyre proffude deuocion wyth many teres mykel afflyccion spekynge thynkynge doynge alweye coude myghte pleysyng god saye oute take holy grace thorugh whiche halowed moders wombe ferthermore lady sayd wete thou wel certayne cometh grace mannes soule prayer bodyly affliccion haue yeuen god tho thynges may though ben lytyl fewe cometh soule bryngyng hym grete hyhe yeftes grace semeth soule faylled self leseth mynde thynketh euer saide dyde ony thynke pleysynge god semeth owne syght foule wretchyd euer sentece coteyned forsayd reuelacons also seynt jerome wrytynge hir lyf seith manere blessid mayden mary ordeined self maner rule lyuyng fro morn tyde tierce ef daye gaf hir prayer fro tierce none occupied hir bodily weuyng werke efte fro none wete fro prayer augel god come apperid hir who hand toke mete bodyly sustinauce fited algate better werke loue god befel fouden wakyng firste wysdom god lawe cunynge mekenes moost lowe songe psalmes dauyd moost conuenyent semely charite mnost gracyous clennesse moost clene maner vertue moost parfyghte sadde inuariable terforth d profyted alwaye better better none euer saw herde hyr wrothe hyr speche full grace god knowen tonge contynuelly dwellynge prayer lore goddes lawe algate ly aboute hyr felawes none hem sholde trespace syne ony word yt none shold lawhe dyssolutely also none hem sholde offende thorugh pryde ony wronge euer withoute fayllynge blessyd god leste per chaunce ony gretynge praysynge shold letted ro louyng god tyme ony grete hyr answerd ageyne deo gracias t say thanked god wherfor hyr sprange fyrste tyme holy men ben greted layne ageyne deo gracias sayd fedde mete tooke augels hand mete tooke bisshop temple gaf poure men euery daye goddes aungel spake hyr al shold derworth syster moder serued obeyssaunt hyr thus mykel seyth saynt jherome lyf p ferthermore hyr xiiii yere blessyd mayden mary wedded joseph reuelacion god thene wente home ageyne nazareth wryten processe story hyr natiuite thus mykel tyme suffyseth haue mynde cotemplacion tho thynges befellen incarnacion whiche soo wylle wel thynke haue deuoutly mynde folowe vertuously dede shall fynde hem ful ghostly fruyte come speke incarnacon oure lorde jhesu p incarnacon jhesu feste annuncyacion gretynge aue maria capitulu circum whanne plente tyme grace come whiche hyghe trynyte ordeyned saue mankynde dampned thorugh syne adam grete charyte hadde mankynde spyrynge hym hys grete mercy also prayer instauce blessyd spyrytes heuene blessid mayden mary wedded joseph gone home nazareth fader heuene callyd hym archauge gabriel sayd hym thys manere goo dere doughter marye spouse joseph whyche moost chere v creature erthe saye hir blessyd sone hath coueyted hyr shappe hyr beaulte chosen hyr hys moder therfore praye hyr receyue hym gladly hyr haue ordeyned hele sauacyon makynde wylle forgete foryeue wronge hath done hym byfore take hede ymagyne ghoostly thynge bodyly thynke thyne herte thou presente syghte blessyd lord benigne gladde semblaunce speketh wordes syde gabriel lykynge face gladde chere vpon knee knelynge drede reueretly bowynge receyueth message lord soo anone gabriel risyng vp gladde ocoude toke flight fro highe heuen erthe moment mane lykenes vyrgyne mary hyr pryue chambre tyme closed prayer hyr meditacons peraueture redyng prophecie ysaye touchyng incarnacon yet also swyftely flew ernard lord come fonde holy trimen messager thou shalt vnderstonde thys blessid incarnacion hyhe werke holy trinite though hit persone sone incarnate become man beware thou erre imaginacon god holy trinite supposynge thre persones fader sone holy ghost ben thre erthely men thou feest thy bodyli eye whiche ben thre dyuerse substauces eche departed fro none hem nay thys ghostly substuce holy trynyte tho thre persones ben one substauce one god yet ther none persones yet may thou vnderstode mane reason ne conceyue thy bodyly wytte therfore take generall doctrine mater algate tyme thou herest thynkest trynyte godhede ghoostly creature aungels soules whiche yu mayst see propre kynde thy bodyly eye ne fele thy bodyly wytte studye fer mater occupye thy wytte therwith thou woldest vnderstode bodyly reson wylle whyle thys boisto body lyuyng erthe therfore whan thou herest ony suche thyng byleue passeth thi kindely reson trowe soth fastly soth holy chirche techeth goo ferther thou shalt bileue thys mater incarnacon second persone trynyte goddes sone henene come erthe tooke flesshe blood blessyd vyrgyne mary become veray man yet neuer departed fro fader holy ghost godhede euer dwelling stylle hem one god heuen goo oure purpos incarnacion sayd take hede haue mynde thou present pryue cha er af lady holy trynyte present aungel gabriel lorde hows suche ghestes ben suche thynges ben done though holy trynyte euer presece god hede neuertheles thou maist thynke vnderstonde special maner reson hys hyhe werke incarnacion gabriel entred mary chambre stoken fro men fro aungels saynt bernard sayth knelynge wyth reuerence beganne message wordes said heyle ful grace oure lord blessyd thou wymen aboue wymen mary herynge message thys newe gretynge neuer herd astonyed abasshed nought answerde thought gretynge thys myghte abasshet troublet ony vycious synfull distourblynge ne agaste presence wonte aungels presence syghte hem gospel sayth astonyed worde newe gretynge neuer wonte fore grete maner moche gretynge sawe self comended praysed specially thre grete thynges yt parfyghtely meke must nedes abasshed hyhe gretynge commeded sul grace oure lord blessyd aboue wymen moche parfyyte meke maye praysynge withoute abasshement shamefastnes therfore abasshed astonyed wyth honeste shamefastnes also drede though trowed wel augel said sothe neuertheles drede word mykel ben parfytely meke haue propirte rewarde owne vertues rather taken hede owne defaultes thorugh mowen gate profyte vertuously holdyng hem self grete vertue lytyl lytyl defaulte grete wyse shamefast dredeful helde pee ansuerd mayst thou take ensample mary fyrst loue lytary prayer departyng fro men thou mayst worthy aungels presence ferthermore lore wisdome thou speke kepe scylece loue lytyl speche ful grete proutfytable vertue marye herde firste aungel twyes speke wold answere one ageyne therfore hit abhominable thyng grete repreef mayden vyrgyne grete iangler namely relygyous ferthermore gospel au gel beholdyng semblauce knowynge cause hir abasshemente drede answerd hir thoughte spake homely callynge hyr name sayd drede thou marye thou abasshed ashamed praysing haue grete trouthe thou arte ful grace thy self also thou hast founden speciall grace god recouerd grace al mankynde bernar loo thou shalt coceyue bere chylde thou shalt calle name jhesus betokeneth sauyour shall saue fro synne dampnacon al peple trewely hopen hym p sayth saint bernard god graute lord jhesus vouchesauf nombre amonge peple saue fro synnes sothely drede manynot shewen hem peple whiche knoweth ne hath people drede maye saye many semen peple religyous holy people worshippeth wyth lyppes sothely herte ful ferre fro wolt thou knowe thou peple wylt thou people yt lord jhesus bydeth ye gospel lawe prophetes also byddeth mynystres bebernar buxome vykers ben holy chirche thy soueraines good wel lyuynge also shrewes euylle lyuynge lerne jhesu meke herte buxome shalt blessyd peple ferthermore aungel speketh praysynge thys childe jhesus shall grete temporal lordship worldly dygnyte shall forsake shal grete god man grete prophete myracles wyrchyng grete doctour sothfaitenes prechyng grete coquerour myghtely deuylle ouercomynge worthyly shal cleped sone ther hyest lorde god whiche shall ye e hym sete da id fader shall take mankynde borne flesshe desete aucestrye shall regne hous jacob euermore kingdome shal none ende hous jacob ghostly holy chirche whiche jhus shall reygne trewe soules fyrst ouercomyng synnes deuylle erthe grace heuen blysse withouten ende may thou say saynt bernard desyrynge kigdome jhu thus come lord jesu putte aweye al sclauders ynne fro thy reame soule soo thou maye reygne therein oweth couetyse cometh chalengeth reame presumpcyon coueyteth lorde pryde wolde quene lechery saith wol regne de traccion enuy wrath glotony stryuen whiche hem shal pricipally regne mykel wa e ageynstonde hem thou lord jhesu destroye hem thy vertue take thou thy reame thy kyngdome haue trewe kyng thy lord jhesu whan aungel hadde tolde condicions worthynes blessid child meke mayden mary chosen mo der spake fyrste aungel nought dredyng wordes ne hyr coceyuyng ne knoulechyng ne forsakyng praysynges said gretynge wyllynge certyfyed playnly drede sholde lese hir maydenhede asked augel maner hyr conceyuynge wordes maner shal done syth knowe man flesshely haue made vowe kepe chaste lord god withoute faylle shalle neuer dele wyth man flesshly aungel answerd said hir shal done wyrchynges holy ghost shal lyghten synguler maner thoruy vertu alther hygest thou shalt coceyue sauyng thy maidenhede therfore holy thyng shall borne shal named godes sone coforte ferthermore aungel said loo elizabeth thy cosyn olde bareyne hath coceyued child six monethes apassed ther shal thyng imposible god take good hede haue mynde fyrst holy trynyte abydinge fynal answer asset blessyd vyrgyne mary takyng hede holdyng lykyngly hir shamefast seblaunce hir sadde manersbernar hir wyse wordes ferthermore blessyd spyrytes heuen al ryghtwys lyuynge men erthe alle chose soules tyme helle adam abraham dauyd desyreden hyr assente stode sauacion mankynde also augel gabriel stodynge reuerence lady enclynyng mylde semblaunce abydeth answer hys mesage syde take hede mary stant sadly drede mekenes grete auysement hauyng pryde ne veyne glorye al hyhe praysynge said tho souerayne yeftes grace hath herde yeuen hir neuer yeue creature aretid grace god lerne yu ensaple hir shamefaste vertuously meke withouten two vertues mayde bernar hede vyrgynyte lytyl worthe saynte bernarde saith vyrgynyte fayre vertue mekenes mor necessary thou may sauf wythoute fyrst withoute mekenes thou maye soo moche dar hardly saye withoute mekenes vyrgynite mary plesynge god mary meke ye holy ghost rested vpon hir sayth saynte bernard ye last ende gospel seith mylde mayde mary herde wysely vnderstonde aungels wordes good auysement yaf hir assente thys maner writen reuelacons knelyd doun souerain deuocion holdyng vp bothe hir handes lyftyng vp eyen heuen sayd wordes loo handmayden sone entrid hir wombe thorugh worchyng ye holy ghost made flesshe blod taken body chyldren conceyued borne kynde ben shapen membre membre soule shedde body anone fyrste instaunce full shapen membres nyght toke wey toward egypte fledde grete lord pursute seruaut ye propirly deuyls seruaunt trauayllynge hym yonge tendyr moder old man jhseph noyo wey hard dyuerse inhabited also wey long say comyn nyghtes waye foude ful seldome ony hous ought haue inwardly copassion hem loth thynke trauellous doo penauce self sythen took soo grete ofte trauaylle v namely noble soo worthy also thys processe yf fader almyghty nede hit thy blessid sone flee thou myytest defende hym fro hys enemyes kepe hym sauf also tribulacion dysease soo moche hem behoueth goo soo ferre londe knewe hard weyes noyous sythen soo mykel vndisposed goynge trauayllyng oure lady yongth tendyrnes joseph also elde feblenesse also child shold bere carye vnnethes two monethes olde yet yeden londe whiche poure vnknowe helpe hem delyte bynethe erthely thynges soo mykel ageyne departed fro loue aboue heuenly godly thynges p also one thre whyche worlde isquinta racio infecte synne foule luste eyen suche curiositees seruen nought ellys fede eyen ofte man lykyngly vayne wyth suche curiositee fedeth eyen soo ofte maker vser offendyth god wherfore men sholde eschewynge suche curiositees yeuynge occasion synne man shold assente synne ony cause manere absteyne fro thesexta racio offeuse god sythen oure lorde yafe ensample comendeth loneth pouerte oft sayd wythout doubte foloweth gretely offendyd thynge directe contrary pouerte specially curiositee also al harmes ouer tokensep racio septimu malum vayne lyghte vnstable herte foule wherfore wylle lyue clennesse conscience withoute de fylynge soule hym behoueth absteyne hym bothe fro makynge also fro vsynge suche vayne curiositees flee fro fro venemous serpete neuer theles thys forsayd repreef curiosite shal vnder stande generally forbeden make fayre werkes honeste apparaille leeful soo hit kepe good meane namely thynges werkes longen goddes seruyce whiche hit nedeful beware eschewe corupte entente vayne joye fals affeccion foule lykynge worldes vanite soo vertuous meane suffysaunt honeste passe excesse vicio curiosite thus mykel suffyseth seid mater tyme p tornynge ageyne lorde jhesu fro egypte capitulum vndecunum herode dede seuen yere ende whyche oure lord jhesus dwellyd egypte aungel oure lord appiered joseph slepe badde sholde take chylde hys moder god londe israel dede soughten chylde slee anone rose vp chylde moder aungel badde torned ageyne londe israel p came herde archelaus sone herode regned partye cleped judea dradde durste goo thyder efte boden aungel slepe wente countre galylee cyte nazareth p maye see comynge ageyne jhesu hit goynge sayd drede disease medled comforte ease tyme beynge straunge londe herde dethe enemyes shold come ageyne owne lande noo doubte yt grete coforte hope ease takynge hede therwith harde trauaylle waye whan comen owne londe hope pee tydynges newe enemye drede hym abyden eschewe countrey discomforte disease alle oure lorde hit sayde lord jhesu thou fayre yonge chylde thou arte lorde kyng heuen erthe dysease trauaylle suffredest thou onre sake soone thou beganst sothely well spake prophete youre persone whan seyd thus p poore dyuerse trrauaylles fro mypauper sum go fyrste yongthe swete jhesu yedest thou caryed alle longe hard waye namely thorugh horryblae deserte passynge ouer rede see also flode jordan tendyr age hit semyth ageyne comyng trauayllous noyous thy leders thy honestely fro hous hous askynge sawe ye ouyt sone sawe ye ouyt sone vnnethes myyt fele hir self sorowe care hir sone sely olde man joseph folowed hir algate wepyng tyme hadden longe souyten fouden hym rest hope hadden nyyt namely moder loued hym moost tendirly sothly wonder though hadden coforte al thouy frendes coforted hem myyten lytyll losse lese jhesu wherfore maye haue resonably grete compassion grete anguysshe ladyes soule hir sone neuer grete sorowe fro tyme borne also may lerne tyme tribulacons anguisshe falle v heuy mykel distourbled therby sithen god spared owne moder thys party sustreth generally tribulacions falle ben chose ben token loue v expediente haue hem many skylles thene lady sory said myght fynde hir sone nyght closed hir cha bre toke hir prayer best remedy caas sayeng maner almyghty fader heuen full mercyo io pyte hit lyked yow youre wylle yeue dere sone loo fader haue lost hym wote thou knowest thynge telle shewe swete sone yeue hym agayn good fader take hede beholde sorowe herte grete necligence knowleche wel haue offendyd caas neuertheles falle ignoraute ye grete goodnes yeue hym ageyn may lyue withoute hym thou swete sone ihu arte thou arte thou herberowed lord whether thou goon vp heuen ageyne thy fader wote wel thou arte god goddes sone thene woldest thou telle also wote wel thou arte veray man borne kepte bare ye egypte fro malyce herode sought slee whether ony wycked man hath aspyed fader heuen almyghty kepe shylde fro alle perylle malyce dere sone telle thou arte may come el thou come foryeue neclygence thys tyme behete shal neuer efte befalle befalle wote neuer thou knowest arte hope lyf al good withoute maye lyue maner suche wordes maye deuoutely suppose nyghte moder cared prayed hyr dere sone vpon morowe erly mary joseph soughten hym dyuerse wayes den jherusalem ferthermore soughten hym besely amonge frendes kynnesme myyte hym wherfore moder sory myyte maner comforted thirde daye whan comen jherusalem soughten inwardly wepinge joye also soone chylde jhesus sawe moder wente hyr vnspekable joye clypped hym armes kyssynge hym ofte sythes holdynge hym barme rested whyle hym tendernes tyll take spyryte thenne spake hym sayd dere sone hast yu done v maner lo thy fader grete sorowe haue soughte al thre dayes thene answerde ageyn said eyleth seche knowe ye wel behoueth occupyed tho thynges longen worshyp fader wordes vnderstode yt tyme thene said moder sone wylte thou goo home ageyn v mekely answerynge said wylle doo ye wylle doo pleasyng yow soo subget hem wente home ageyne hem vnto theyr cyte nazareth p thys forsaid processe jhesu hope dyde maner lyued tho thre dayes may suppose wete somed hospytale poore men shamefastly prayed asked herborow ete laye wyth poore men poore chylde doctoures sayen begged thre dayes therof lytel force folowe hym innota parfyte mekenes vertues beggynge without forth meke herte within forth lytel worth perfeccion ferthermore forsaid processe maye note lerne forti witnessyth wherfore tyll come degre perfeccon shall holde oure self ful imparfyte ne nought acounte fythen sothenesse done vnworthy sernauntes tyme done good owe doo god hym self witnessyth till tyme come degre abieccon parfyte repreef self ben sette sadly trouth rather vanyte ye apostle openly sheweth wordes holdeth hym self owne reputacion ought worthyqaise quid esse sythen sothenesse nought begyleth deceyueth hym self saide oure lord jhesus lyued maner made hym self abiecte vnworthy world owne nede teche v true way perfeccon wherfor yf lerne may ercused abhomynable thynce see hym togyder euery daye one lytyl borde precious delicate mete symple sobre oonly nedeful sustenauce kynde mete speken gyder also paraueture mete vayne wordes dissolute wordes deuocon ful wysdome holy ghoost soo en fedde body mykel better fedde soule thene suche maner recreacion comyn wenten prayer theym self theyr closettes maye ymagyne noo grete hous lytyl whyche thre seuerynges hit thre smal chabres specially pranota ye slepe maye thynke lord jhs criste euery nyght prayer gooth bedde lowely mekely shewynge nedes mankynde man hydynge godhede fro fende lord jhesu wel mayste thou cleped hydde god woldest thys longe tyme thus trauaylle putte penauce moost innocet body oure sake whan trauaylle one nyght suffysed redempcion world thy grete loue man made doo grete dedes penauce hym thou art kynge kynges almyghty god wyth oute ende helpest men theyr nede yeuest thy go ode plentyuously euery condycon state asnota r ca na l u dal keth ye chose reserued youre owne persone soo grete pouerte abieccon penauce wakyng slepyng absteynynge etynge youre dedes doynge longe tyme oure loue lord god ben louen soo mykel lust lykynge ease flesshe se soo besely precious curious dyuerse ornamentes vanytees worlde sothely louen desyren suche thynges lerne scole mayster taughte v bothe worde dede mekenesse pouerte penaunce chastysynge body sythen ben wyser yf wylle erre lette v folowe hym souerayne mayster wyll begyle maye begyled also doctryne hys apostle hauige lyuelode clothyng apayed nede couenable superfluyte also vertuous lyuynge exercyses sayd folowe oure power oure lorde jhesu maye wrechid lyf penaunce come blysse lyf euerlastyng joye amen p baptisme oure lorde jhesu waye therto capitulum xiiii nyne twenty yere complete whiche oure lord jhesus lyued penaunce ab eccion sayd begynynge xxx yere spake thys moder saide dere moder hit tyme goo gloryfye fader make hym knowen also shewe self ye world wyrke sauacion ne sonle fader hath ordeyned sente worlde ende wherfore good moder good coforte shall soone come ageyne therwith souerayne maister mekenes knelyng downe moder asked lowely blessyng also knelynge clyppynge hym derworthly hir armes wepyng said thus blessid sone thou wolt goo thy faders blessyng myn thynke haue minde soone come ageyne soo reueretly takynge leue moder also supposed fader joseph took way fro nazareth ward jherusalem soo forth tyl came water jordan iohn baptysed peple tyme whyche place fro jherusalem space eyghte myle lord al world gooth longe way bare foote allone yet none disciple gadred wherfore takynge good entente inward copassion hym iourney speke hym deuoutly herte thynkynge edi uot nota maner lord jhu ye ben kynge kynges whyder goo ye maner alone good lord ben duke erles knyghtes baron horse harneys chari ottes somers seruauntes mynystres shold aboute kepe fro comyn peple maner kynges lordes ben trompes clario ne mynstralsye herbegers purueyours shold goo al worshippes pompes world wretchyd wormes vse ye hye lorde who joye blysse heuen erthe replenysshed thene goo ye thus symply alone bare erthe sothely ye cause ye thys tyme kyngdome whiche worlde ye haue auauntysed youre self takynge maner seruaut kynge soo ye haue made youre self one v na p r g go sum si cut omn ri pylgryme stranger al oure faders ye come seruaunte make v kynges sholde sykerly come youre reame ye come youre self shewynge v true waye wherby sholde mowe come vp lorde god leue forsake waye folowe n r b u mund l ot lowe meke oure self loue holde coueyte soo besely worshippes pompes vanytees worlde sothely oure reame thy worlde knowe self pylgrymes straugers therfore fallen al folyes myscheues soo vayne men sone louen holden aldaye thynges ben vayn fals tho ben good true tho ben temporel euer fayllynge tho ben heuenly euerlastyng truly gode lord yf desyren sadde youre reame co forte heuenly thynges also therwyth yf inwardly thoughten knewen self pilgrymes stranger shold soone lyghtely folowe erthely teporel goodes takynge oonly nedeful lyuynge shold taryed renne yow wythouten byrthen shold goo lyghtely fully despyse sette nouyt wordly rycheses goodes speke ferthermore baptysme lord jhesu tyme come water jordan founde johan baptysynge synfull men mykel peple come thyder predicacon helden hym tyme cryste thene oure lorde jhesus amonge wente johan prayd hym wolde baptyse hym johan beholdynge hym knowynge hym spiryte adred grete reuerece said lord shold baptysed thou comest answerd suffre thus falleth besemeth v fulfille ryghtwysnesse saith saye thys bewreye make knowe tyme therof yet come doo bydde baptyse p ota tee g du hu unlitati tyme mekenes therfore wyll fulfille al maner mekenes saith glose mekenes hath thre degree first degree man subget lowed souerayn preferred hyed hym self aboue hym euen hym astate secod subget euen lyke astate hyed preferred aboue vnderlinge thirde souerayn degree mekenes subget lowed vnderlyng lasse astate tha degree kepte lord ihs time wha meked hym lowed hym johan therfore fulfilled ryghtwysnes perfeccion mekenes thenne whan johan sawe lordes must nedes doo dyde ba baptysed hym take goode hede hye lord mageste despoilleth hym oth clothes another symple man peple plonged colde water colde tyme wynter al loue hele ordeynyng sacrament baptisme wasshyng therwyth none owne synes f none oure fylthes oure synes weddynge ghostly hym holy chirche generally trewe soules scylence thynketh thou hast longe tyme holde thy pee ye ful longe speke thou hast leue ye fader longe wolt thou art vertu god wisdom fader hyd peple feble vnconyng longe thou art worthy kynge heuen fro knowyng men whether dradde ought vayne joye shold drede vayne joye sothenesse joye fader neuertheles drede hym felf v whiche knewe wel nede adredde vayne joye spake mouthe taught v dede thynge chapitre lord jhesus mekely helde pee tyme doctryne flee presumcon kepe parfyte mekenes whiche vertue yet baptisme shewed growe souerayne lowenes opely shewed seruaut makynge hym worthy grete hym self vnworthy abiecte also nother poynte may see mekenes growen tyme sayd lyued lowely ydelnesse abieccon shewed hym self openly synful man johan preched synful men doo penauce baptised oure lord jhs came amonge syght baptysed one souerayne poynte mekenes namely tyme wha purposed preche shewe self goddes sone way mane reason shold haue drede thene lowe dede leest therby whene preched shold haue ben lesse reputacon dispysed synful vnworthy therfore lefte mayster mekenes meke hym self al maner lowenes doctryne ensaple shewyng hym self thyng despyte abieccion hym self contrarynota contra supe b maner shewen self ben worship praysynge self yf ony thynge v vertue ought preysed gladly shewen maken knowe oure defaultes trespaces helen hyden yet sothenes wyked synful thoughn soo knowen self oure owne syght vnworthy synful neuertheles wold beholde syght oure mekenes ferre fro parfyte mekenes jhesu shewed dedes shewed vertu moost nedeful v wherfore loue hit besye v oure dedes pryncipally kepe hit dredynge therby vnable profyte tymenota souerayne mekenes vnderfongynge hys baptysme taken seruaunt shewed wytnes fader token ye holy ghost goddes sone soo though make v abiecte lowe v neuer mykel owne syyte menes yf able profyte god make v knowen tyme hit moost spedeful oure owne mede menes prouffyte amen p explicit par secunda et contemplacio pro die marti p incipit par tercia p fastynge oure lorde jhesu temptacions deserte p capitulum xv tyme oure lord jhesus baptysed said anone went deserte vpon hill fro place baptisme aboute foure myle cleped quaretana fasted xl dayes xl nyytes etynge drynkyng ye euangeliste marke telleth dwellynge beestes yeue good entente lord jhu specially dedes techeth v yeueth v ensample many grete vertues yt solytary fasteth prayeth waketh lyeth slepeth vpon erthe mekely conuersaut beestesnota bene cessum dequatuor ye whiche processe ben towched foure thynges lo gen specially ghostly excercise vertuo lyuynge wonder fully helpynge eche togyder say solytary beynge fastyng prayer penauce body whiche wepu ta cordio may come best yt noble vertu clennesse herte whiche owe soueraynly desyre moche moost nedeful v coprehendeth self vertues manere say charyte mekenes pacience alle vertues also putteth awaye vyces vice wyth defalute vertues clennes herte may stode laste therfore book cleped collaciones patrum sayd al excercise monke sholde pryncypally gete haue clennesse herte noo wonder therby man shall deserue see god cryste hym self witnessyth gospel sayenge thus blessid clene herte bernard shall see god sainte bernard saith clenner man nerer god clerelyprimum secundu tercium jeiunium afflictio corporio seeth hym wherfore gete haue noble vertue saye clennesse herte princypally helpeth besy deuoute prayer whiche shall speke mykel prayer glotenye lust lykynge body ydelnes lytyll worthe therfore hit behoueth therwith fastyng bodyly penauce discrecion bodily penauce without discrecon letteth al gode werkes also kepynge fulfyllynge tho thre sayd thynges helpeth moche fourth solytary beynge moche noise troublynge praier well deuoutly said seeth hereth many thynges shal ful hard escape vnclennesse hert offence coscience ofte sythes deth entreth wyndowes soule wherfo thou wilt knytte ghostly lord jhesu criste coueytest clennesse herte see god ensample hym goo solytary place moche thou mayst sauynge thyne astate flee copany flesshely seche curiosite newe knowleche freshippes fylle thyn eyen thyn eres vayn fantasyes withoute cause holy faders soughten desertes solitary place fer fro comyn couersacion men also nouyt taughten boden hem dwelleden religious couersacon shold blynde dee dombe may lette distourble rest soule flee venemous soule solitary beyng fleyng bernard say sayth vertuously soule body say yt man entencion deuocion spiryte departed fro ye world men ioyned spyryte god spyryte asketh solytary beynge body maner tyme specially tyme special prayer also tyme hem owen way degree solytary recluse relygious therfore saith saint yu art amonge many bodyly men thou maist solytary alone ghostly yf thou loue worldly thynges ye comynalte loueth also yf thou despyse forsake tho thynge comynly al men desyre taken also yf thou flee stryues debate yf thou fele sorewe thyn owne harmes haue mynde wronges done ye auengyd el though thou allone solytary body thou arte allone soule truly p generally manere companye men thou arte couersaut beware specially thoo thynges yf thou wilte truly solytary spirite thou curious besy sercher menes conuersacyonor el presumtuouse temerary demer men saynte bernardes sentence solytary beynge whiche may vnderstade bodyly solicitude suttyseth oute ghostly haue ghostly bodily helpeth ful moche puttynge away occasion without forth myyt drawe ioule within forth fro onynge knyttynge hir spouse jhesu crist wherfore maye knytte hym grace aboute wille myght tolowe hym saye true solitary beynge layde deuoute prayer fastyng discrete bodily penau ce doyng ferthermore couersacon deserte wasnota ne amonge bestes haue ensample lyue symply bere v lowely congregacion ben bere paciently suffre also hem semen v vure sonable bestiall maneres lyuynge thus hauyng mynde maner lyuynge lord jhu crist deserte penauce tho xl dayes euery crysten soule ought visite hym oftymes deuoute copassion specially tyme begynyng epiphanye baptised xl dayes whiche fasted lyued sayd ferthermere teptacion whan tho xl dayes fastynge coplete oure lord jhs hongred andde ep ci one prima temptaco de gul anone fals temptour fende besy boute knowe whether wer goddes sone came hym began tempte hym glotonye sayd yf thou goddes sone saye stone made tornyd loues myghte trechery deceyue hym maister trouthe answerd hym soo wysely neyther ouercome temptacion glotenye yet aduersary myghte knowe desyred neyther denyed ne affermed goddes sone cocluded hym auctoryte holy wrytte soo haue ensapie lord jhesu withstonde vyce glotenye must begynne yf wylle ouercome vycesde enemy comynly begyneth therwyth assaylle hem taken hem ghostly lyuynge wherfore semeth ouercomen vyce gloteny feble vnmyghty withstonde ouercome vyces doctoures sayen place gospel glotony fyrste refrayned man trauaileth vayne agenst vyces afterward deuylle took hym vp bare hym jherusalem fro place aboute eyghte myle men sayen sette hym vpon pynacle temple tempted hym vayne joye coueitynge knowe dyde whether goddes sone also ouercome auctoryte holy writte loste fully purpoos hurte hym man pryde hym self neuer vyser hys godhede haue ensample pacience cosiderynge grete benygnyte pacience oure lorde jhesu suffred hym self handeled borne cruel beest hated hym loued tyme saynt bernard sayth enemy seyng shewed noo thynge godhede supposynge therby god tempted hym man thys thyrdde tyme whenne tooke hym efte bare hym ageyne ful hye hille besyde forsayd hylle quaretana space two myle tempted hym auaryce therwith ydola trye therfore openly repreued fully ouer come vaynquysshed ouercome dyuerse doctoures tellen expowne plainly temptacions thysnota de gospel therfore passe ouer shortlyer doo exposicions standynge pryncipally meditacions said begynnynge thys book take good hede oure lorde handled tempted enemy shold wonder though wretch ben ofte sythes tempted oonly tempted thre tymes also saint bernard saith dyuer se tymes apostle saith tempted maner temptacyou longeth infirmyte man wythoute syne ferthermore whan enemy fully ouercome gone away angel comen serueden mynystreden hymmeditacio uo take good hede beholde inwardly oure lorde jhesu etynge alone augels aboute hym thynke deuoutely ymagynacion tho thynges folowen herafter ben ful faire styrynge deuocon fyrste maye aske maner mete aungels serueden hym longe fast herof speketh holy wrytte wherfore maye ymagyne reason ordeyne worldly feest v lyketh errour affermynge deuoutly ymagynynge supposyng comyn kynde manhede yt take hede speke myghte godhede question doubte myght make hym lyst also haue tho ben made plucked eeres corne eten hem honger shal folowe herafter p also tyme hym self wery way satte vpon welle spekynge woma samarytane rede made mete ete sende disciple cyte begge mete lyckly thys tyme fast bodily honger purueyed mete miracle fythen thys tyme shewed oonly manhede also peple therfore wyrche myracle edificacion comynly dide oonly aungels present sythen hylle noo dwellynge men ne mete redy thynke deuoutly manere tyme sathanas reproued fals temptour vtterly dryuen away holy aungels grete multitude come oure lord jhesu vyctory fallynge downe erthe deuoutely honoured hym salued hym theyr lord almyghty god oure lord benyngly swettely ok hem vp enclynyng hem hede hit knowlechyng hym self veray man somwhat lasse lowed fro augels thene speken augels sayde thus oure worthy lord ye haue longe fasted youre tyme ete youre wille ordeyne thene said goo forth dere moder maner mete hath redy brynge none bodyly mete lykynge hir dyghtynge anone two theim goynge forth sodeynly hir grete reuerence gretynge hir hir sone behalfe tolde message symple mete ordeyned hir self joseph aungels token loof wel necessaryes broughten hit jhesu perauenture smale fysshes oure lady ordeyned thene god wold therwyth aungels comynge spradden towel vpon grounde leiden brede theron myldly stoden sayden grace oure lord jhesu abydynge blessyng tyl sette p take govide solitarie resluse od entente specially thou arte solytary haue mynde thou etest thy mete alone withoute mane teliship maner mete lowely oure lorde jhes sytteth downe mete bare groude neyther bancquerre ne quysshen take hede hown curteysly sobirly taketh mete notwithstondynge honger longe fast angel serueden hym lord perauenture one brede another wyne another dyyt fysshes songen stede mynstrelsy swete songe heuen soo reheteden couforted lord longen mykel joye medled copassion teliship hast thou though thou see hem whan thou etest allone thy celle yf thou charite specyally thou hast thy herte god ye owe haue byddynge apostle whiche saith v whether eten drynken ony thynge doo shall doo name oure lord whyche name jhesus shall algate blysse thanke hym herte haue mykel haue lytyl haue good haue badde soo ete oure mete though ben alone though seene bodyly blessyd aungels ben presente ghostly hauynge inward compassion oure lorde jhesu beholdynge mynde hym almyghty god souerayne lorde maker alle worlde yeueth mete alle jordan johan baptiste soone sawe hym come towarde hym wyth fynger puttynge toward hym shewed hym sayd loo lambe god loo dooth way synes worlde hit vpon whome sawe holy ghost reste tyme baptysed hym p afterward also nother day whan johan hadde shewed hym dyde firste andrewe peter disciple speken wyth hym hadden begynnynge knowleche johan telleth gospel afterward oure lord jhes lefte countre took soueraynly fair also moost eloquente dauid saith hym also thou faire shappe passyng chyldren specio pre homi num grace shewed thy lyppes ferthermore also lord jhesus besyenge hym aboute oure sauacon sauf luke maketh mynde twelue apostle chosen nameth hem take good entent manere hym thys clepyng gadryng hys dicyples hys conuer sacion wyth hem lowely speketh homely sheweth hym self drawynge hys loue wythinforth grace wythoute forth dede famyliarly ledyng hem hys moders hous also going wth hem ofte dwellynges techyng enformynge hem soo alle manere beyng besy aboute hem wyth grete cure line moder hath hyr owne sone soo mykell wryten saynt peter tolde tyme slepte wyth hem ony place hys custome ryse vp nyght hem slepyng yf fonde ony vnhyled preuely softely hyled hym ageyne loued hem ful zebedee shapte wedde sone john yede oure lady nazareth fro chane aboute four myle saieng wolde make brydale sone john soo thenne oure lady wente wyth hir ordeine therfore certayne dayes soo ghestes defaulte wyne tolde preuely sone therof helpe remedy myght haue yf hadde sette amonge wymen rysen fro borde semely also leue vertuously shamfaste sat ne among men wherfore foloweth satte gheste mynystred sayd p thyrde euydence herof bad seruautes goo hyr ne sholde badde semeth ouer hem brydale gouerned hyr therfor besy default wherfore may take hede vnderstande maner thys brydale processe myracle therat done thus fyrste shall beholde lord jhesu etynge amonge hem another comyn man syttynge lowest place amog grete worshypful ghestes abouen may ond er stande thys processe shold teche thys lesson gospel whanthow arte beden brydale feste sytte take thy stede loweste place mykel wold firste doo dede sholde teche woord therfore wolde take first pryncipall sete maner prowde men rather lower amonge symple p also behold lady moder yt al thynge wel couenably done tellynge seruautes mynystres sholde serue wherof p soo whan drowe toward ende feste comen hyr saiden wine aswered abydeth litil shall gete haue wente cha bre hall sone jhesus satte atte bordes ende nyhe cahmbers dore rownyd hym ere saye dere sone haue noo wyne thys syster poure wherfore ne wete shal haue jhesus aswered said woman thys seme hard bostous answere hys moder neuerthe lesse sayd mystery ductryne techynge saint bernarde sayth shall tolde processe hard strauge answere semynge hys moder distourbled ne despeyre fully trustynge grete godenes benignite wente ageyne seruau te sayd gooth sone jhesus euer sayth byddeth doth byd dyng lord fylleden stenes ful water anone hys blessyng water tornyd wyne thenne badde drawe therof bere archetryclyne saye moost worthy persone alle hgestes hous whyche byddyng may see fyrste dyscrecyon lorde sente wyne fyrste moste worshypfull man also maye see lorde satte fere fro hym sayd bereth hyt archetryclyne sythen satte hygeste place semeth oure lorde satte lowest place sayd whan hadde tasted wyne preysed dronken therof mynystres knewen made tolden openly myracle thenne hys dyscyples byleueden hym sadly fyrst myracle seen done hem soo jhesus shewed hys blysse hys godhede p afterward whan este al done lord jhesus called john sayd leue thys woman thou hast taken thy wyf folowe shal bryng better parfyte weddynge thys aone wythoute johan lefte hys wyf folowed jhesus thys forsayd processe may many thynges doctryn edificacion fyrst lord jhesus wold come presente attebrydale weddyng shewed v matrymony flesshely wedding leefful ordeined god called johan ther fro doth v vnd er stonde ghoostly matrymony mikel better perfite worthy also harde answere straunge semynge yaf moder sayd woman saynt bernard sayth taught v ben relygious haue forsake world besy haue grete care flesshely parentes soo theyr nede lette ghostly exercyse long ben worlde longe dette parentes haue left forsake self mykel free delyuerd besinesse hem finde writen ther cam vpon tyme hermite monke forsake worlde lyued solytaryly deserte owen flesshely broder prayeng hym hys helpe certeyne nede touchinge world bade hym go hys broder dede longe afore whanne wondred byddynge sayde dede knewe wel monk answerde sayd washe dede world soo thaught v lord jhsus haue forsake worlde sholde besy aboute oure pareutes flesshely frendes ouer relygyon asketh answered hys moder namely suche moder sayeng woma p anoder vnderstondyng wordes whiche cominly doctoures tellen therfore passe ouer atte tyme ferthermore haue techynge pacience hope dede lady lefte straunge answere sayd soo tyme callen jhesu helpe atte oure nede bodily ghostly though finde anone rather hardnes contrariete shall leue therfore calle vpon hym gode hope tyll thorugh mercy grace vnsauery water cold aduersite penauce torned wyne comforte ghostly lykynge p thys myracle done lord jhesus wyllyng purposynge wyrche preche openly sauacion man wente fro place wyth hys moder hys disciple capharnaum besyde nasareth leding hys moder wey folowyng hys discyples besily heryng wordes techynge ydell dyd wroughte good taughte spake edyfycacyon doo p excellet name blessid without ende ame srmon oure lord jhu made hylle caplm xviii whane lord jhus hadde chosen gadred disciple sayd willynge teche hem enforme hem perfeccion newe lawe ladde hem vp hille called thabor two myle fro nazareth comyn opinion made hem longe sermonaugustin de sermo dni mo ful fruyte whyche saint austin sayth begynnynge boke made sermon conteyneth alle perfeccion cristen liuinge sermon taughte hem fyrste whiche men god ben blessyd worthy haue blysse also taughte hem true maner prayer fastinge almesdede vertues longynge parfite lyf man texte gospel ope ly telleth diuerse doctoures clerkes expounen suffisau tly whiche processe may passe ouer mykel wryten bothe latyn englysshe many place also ful long processe touche al poyntes therof maner meditacon wherfor shal time specially note lord began sermon fyrst de p ta pouerte doyng v pouerte fyrst grou de al gostly excercyse ouerleyd charged withe temporell gode worldly rychesse vertues folowen place gospel mede hem behight come tyme foloweth vertue pouerte behygthe come tyme present yeuen cryste forsayd wordes beginyng sermon ben blessyd tho ben poure spirite mede kingdom heuen lo saith mede shal de also ben pour poure spirite b blessid therin stant vertu pouerte poure spirite hath lytil spirite pryde comyn mankinde fyrst syne man called poure worldly hath lityl worldly good leuynge materb torne v conteplacion beholdyng lord jhu lowely mekely sitteth vpon hill disciple lowely sadde chere speketh thoo wordes ful edificacion teched nobel lesson souerayne perfeccion also mekely entetly disciple beholden blessyd face heren swete wordes setten hem besyly mynde soo haue grete joye ghostly lykynge speche sighte specyally hope comforted nobel shorte praier tauyt hem amonge tyme pater noster grete frute felten therin also grete trust hope put therby maye well suppose firste fruite therof vnderstonde lettir also therwith hadden thorugh grace ghostly vnd er stondyng eche peticion therof sythen ther conteyned askynge al v nedeth body soule touchinge temporel lyf worlde lyf euerlastynge nother world al comprehendid shorte wordes wonder thouy hadden grete likinge comforte praier grete fruyt tasted therin hauen al thorugh grace fele ghostly fruyte swete taste therof p also secondesecundu comforte prayer trust hope might trust hope stabled strengthed see hym al knewe nedeful spedeful hem aske myghte yeue hit hem teche hem petycy whiche myght erre askinge fay le askynge soo dome man made lybelle cause ageynst whyche myght yeue dome sentence p also lorde made bille seruautes aske thoo thynges nede ful likyng graute comforte myght touchinge prayer askyng nede p also ouer comforte prayer mykel nexte place sermon reproued prayer ypocrytes wern wor thy herde soo medecine confortable likinge defaulte sekenes opened tolde fore comforte shall fynde forsayd prayer pater noster yf saye hit deuoutly dedely syne lord jhus made prayer discyples tyme specially hym hille also v al cristen men generally shold make prayer fader heuen name worldes ende causa harme mykel peple deceyued leuen mykel thys moost worthy prayer best singuler de nocion priuate prayer sayeng withoute denocion may see day many men wymmen bering bede trillynge finger waggynge ye lippes syghte caste vanitees herte god knoweth drede sette vpon worldly thynges ye whyche manere peple speketh lord god prophete saith thus peple prayeth honoureth lyppespopulus hic labiis honorat herte fer mykel matere spoken many tretees bokes bothe latyne englysshe prayer sufficautly expouned therfore passen ouer shortly time herof de p ri cia pa no one thynge touchyng prayer sothely trowe whoo wille yeue entente saye wyth deuocion hath inward desire ghostly vnderstonding therof settyng herte mykel may saith comin pryuate shalle thorughe grace processe tyme fynde soo mykel comforte none prayer made man shal hym soo sauery effectuell euer nede caas styred specially pray remedy helpe god soo shall fynde sowle god wyll yeue grace grete likynge diuerse vnderston dynge therof moste aperteyneth hys desyre writen comyn exposicion therof parau ur better tell mykel folke seruautes red men haue wille praye speciall mede coueyten true sone loue plesyng oure fader god heuen setten lik ge besines pryuate prayer made man lady sain heue tha done general praier made god hym self whiche withoute doubte moost plesinge hym spedful v therfor ben deceyued many maners speke sauter seruice holy chirche neuertheles deuoute praiers made god oure lady sayntes ben good said deuocion men stired saye couenable tyme sette affeccion lasse vpon moste worthy prayer pater noster mykell folke sayeng priuate praiers setten entent speken hem grete deuocion sayenge pater noster ben necligent rabben forth withoute deuocion maketh ofte special mede temporel yt hope haue sayenge suche priuate prayer ouercome enemyes kepte fro fyre water sodeyne deth bodely peril grete foly trust vpon ye saieng ony praiers without ritghwys lyuing also men shold desyre suche special temporel medes wylle god knoweth spedful v withoute doubte shal gete v moste effectuelly ony prayer pater noster yf sayd truly wyth deuocion specially peticion askinge fiat volutas tua sicut celo et terra saye oure ader heuen thy wylle doone al thing heuen erthe yf best v kepte fro fyer water sodeyne deth ony bodily perylle wyth oute doubte fader heuen god wylle yeue v forsayd peticion rightwys linyng el saye neuer many priuate prayer rede al daye diuer se martirs saintes brente somme drowned diuerse maners putte shamful dethe worlde best hem encreace joye blisse heuen wherfor ben grete open foly hem may well haue prayed kept fro suche bodily harmes peril ayenst sodeyne deth spedeful many men haue suche dethe shamful mannes syghte saynt gregory telleth ensample prophete abdo woryed lyon god purged tyme ryghtwys men suche shamful dethe holy writjus simo te occupat fu refrige te wytnesseth sothely ryghtwysman yf ouercome ony maner bodely dethe soule shal saued sette reste euerlastynge neuertheles prayen ofte lawfully kepte fro sodayne dethe vnderston de combred wyth dedely synne therinne deye withoute repentauce herte shryfte mouthe therto hope moost beste effectuel prayer pater noster specyally two laste petycyons askinges therof whyche prayen almighty god fader heuen suf freth v falle combred temptacyon dedelyet n ducas p ta syne kepe v delyuere v fro wyckednesse though matere worthy prayer plentiuous also thesyre wryther herof speke neuertheles writen many place hope suffysautly also grete processe foloweth leue matere thys tyme al fructuous sermon lord jhus made discyples hyll goynge downe deuoute contemplacion beholdinge noble lesson taught hyll skylful hyghe per feccion therof lord jhus cam downe meke lke disciple spekyng also homely hem waye chykens hene folowen mikel ghostly lykynge coueytynge eche ne hym vertuous swete wordes p come downe curteis lord jhesus prayed symon leprose daye ete therto grauted gladly came mete wonte oftsythes hys owene curtosie also loue zele hadno de cu al tate dom sauacyon mane sowles wyche made man etyng wyth hem benygnly comining wyth hem drowe hem ye loue hym also mykel made hym self pertitely poure toke none pocession worldly godes hym self hys therfore thruy loue pouerte ye mirrour mekenes time prayed beden mete toke tyme place mekely wyth curtesye thanking gode wyll ne befelle mary maudeleyne parauentur time herde hym preche thorugh touchyng hys grace gretly styred compunction feruent loue hym though hit yet preuely hydde herte whan herde knew mete hous forsayd simon feruetly touched sorow herte inforth synnes also wyth brennynge fyre hys loue myght lenger abyde anone wente forsayd hous jhesus sat mete considryng wythoute hym myght sauf ne haue foryeuenes hir synes went bodely hous foryete hir self taking none regarde ye gestes mete holding doune hir face hir eyen erth letted tyll come hym sought inwardlyno loued lord jhesu anone thene fell doune grounde prostrate hys foot wyth grete inward sorowe shame hyr synnes spake hyr herte hym thynkynge thys manere swete lord wote well truly knowleche yt ye god lorde haue offendyd hyghe mageste many grete offense trespaces mykel knowleche sothely synnes ben wythoute nombre grauell see mykel belyue mercy passeth alle thynge therfor wretchyd synful come flee grete mercy forthynkynge inwardly haue offendid askynge mercy foryeuenes behete herte ame dement synes shall neuer power sake youre obedyence good lord put fro forsake repentauce refute wote well may none haue also wyll haue loue soueraynly aboue alle wherfore gode lorde forsake ye punysshe ye youre wille neuertheles aske algate mercy wyth wyth grete turste hys mercy inward affectyon hys loue kyssede hys feete otfe sadly wepynge shedynge teres thylke shwesshe feete wyth hem semeth yt lord jhesus went bare fote whan wel wepte grete drede hyr vnworthynes hyr here sholde touche hyr lordes fete wiped hym deuoutely borught thing wyth hyr precyous wype also wyped hem wyth hyr heer mendement beofre trespaced hyr heer yt saye hadde vsed pryde vanyte wold put hyt vse mekenes deuocion also feruete loue deuocion yt hym wolde letted therof bi ye fetching ony cloth wipe hem wypyng feete afterwarde de uoutly kissynge hem ofth sythes aoynted hem precious oynement brouyt wyth hyr supposyng pe rauetur oure lordes feete hard weye also inward deuocyon begynnynge wyth drede hys feete dyd boldenes loue anoynted hys hede lord god wold inwardly thinke take hede dede woman circumstauce therof mykel ghostly fruyte sholde fynde theryn sterynge inward repentauce sin ne true loue jhesu grete deuocyon forth processe take hede also maner oure lord jhesu thys tyme benygnly pacyently suffreth hyr doo hyr wylle lyked hym full welle knowynge inward affection true loue hyr herte soo alle tyme seaced etyng also wyth hym ghestes wondryng woman vnkouth dede pacyence oure lord jhesu hys suffrauce specially maister hous simon demed gretely hys herte wolde suffre suche comyn synful woma toche hym homely thought prophete supposyng knew lord passyng prophetes knewe leest thought mane herte answered openly hys preuy thoughtes wyng hym self therby prophete prophete ensample two doctours concluded hym tusty fyeng woman helde synful preued loued hym shewed token loue dede wyth hys feste soo shewynge perfection vertues also justifyeng synfull stant pryncypally true loue god sayd symon conclusyon thus many synes ben foryeuen hyr loued myket thene tourned hym mawdeleyne sayde hir full ende asked thy feyth hath saued goo pee lord jhesu swete lykyng thys word hyr wyth grete joye wente wey sothely lykyng trowe hyt went neuer oute mynde perfytely conuerted jhesu leuyng syne fully lyuynge euer honeste holyly drawen algate hym tono hys moder withoute departyng perseuerautly forsayd processe sentence hys gospel ben many grete notabytees edificacyon whyche woman doth alle truly desyren asken hys mercy behoueth charyte true loue yt specyally commendedca bo hym thys woman ye whcihe pee bitwene god synful man apostle sayth charite couereth multitude synnes withoute whyche inpossyble please god p saynte bernard saith quatite euery man soule shal taken estemed mesure ofbernard su ser vii charyte therin saye soule yt hath mykel charite grete hath lytyl lytyl hath nought nought sayut poule sayth rehersynge many grete vertues concludynge thus haue charyte soothely nought therfor sayth lord thys woman loueth mykyl therfore haddeno mykel foryeuen sayd befor ferthermore also haue ensample true repentaunce penauce isv penitecia peccatis cote lollardos de cote ioe nedful forieuenesse sine shewed woman maudaleyne haue herde whyche penaunce alle hooly chirche techeth stant sorow herte shrift mouthe satisfacton dede parauetur somme men thynkyng fals oppynyon lollardes shryft mouth nedefull sufiseth herte shriue god ye forsayd woma gospell telleth vnkindely lesen grete benefice gaf v manhede wherfore yf wyll restored ageyne knytte hym grace muste doo satisfaction hym god also man haue soo forsake dedely synne manere sayd p soo holy chyrche hath resonably ordeyned beden knowleche mouth make oure confessyon truly oure synne prestes hath specyally ordeyned hys stede hys vykers thoo wordes gospell spake dysciples sayd thus p euer ye bynden erthe shall bonden heuen soo ye vnbynden erthe shall vnbonden heuen p true penaunce nedefull dedely synne repentauce herte also shrifte mouthe preste godes stede yf may lord god afketh therwyth due satisfaccion folowyng haue parfyte ensample opely shewed blessid woman synfull mary maudeleyne processe sayd gospell open ynoughe touchyng firste parte laste saye repentauce satisfaccyon p seconde confession though rede hit hir worde speking nede hym knewe fully herte lord jhu beyng bodily presence sayd neuertheles shewed affeccion confession parfitely dede wold shewe hir hym pryuate synfull askynge mercy myght haue done betwyx hir el discyples sparing shame grete parte penauce confession chese place ye tyme myghte hir open repreef shame hous pharysee whiche knew wel hauynge indygnacion special refusinge haue herd reherced openly tolde hym cam lord jhesu whiche wiste well knewe specyall leste parte therof myght resonably haue reprehended hir openly hade foryeuen curtois lord ful grace mercy sawe contricyon herte gode wyll grounded true byleue god myght fully foryeue hirno fide ate ri quisitis cotricione vera syne hym lyked therwith full hope haue grace foryeuenesse also feruent loue hym whiche thre vertues ben nedefull euery wyll haue foryeuenes syne wythoute ony penauce fully foryaf synes bad goo pee pee coscience fully made bytwene hir god man hir true feyth bilyue whiche grounded parfitely hope charite sayd made hir sauf shall moste synfull man euer shall yf haue truly grounded herte veray contricion thenne withoute doubte wyll spare ony shame knowleche hys syne worde openly man goddesr stede dyde wyll hym bothe god man sayd parauentur semeth men synfull man shall folowe woman true forthin kyng syne shold preste folowe lord lyght foryeuynge shewed therof enioynyng penauce thanr dyde therfore answere holy doctoures sayen contricion forthynkynge synne may grete parfite suffyseth wythoute ony penauce full foryeuenes whyche yf preste myght see fully knowe shold yeue penauce mykel man seeth herte lord jhus god man dyde may knowe party token wythoutforthe therfore syker parte shall enioyne penauce synne lasse holy chirche hath ordeyned wold god synfull people wold folowe woma true forthynkynge thene withn b oute doubte sholde haue god full foryeuynge penauce lesse prestes enioynynge ferthermore forsaid processe gospell oure lorde jhesus yaf ensample prechours goddes worde sholde spare tyme say sothe displesyng hem yt feden hem yeuen hem bodily sustenaunce withstondyng pharisee fedde dyd ofte reprehendyd hym openly owne hous hys mysbileue fals thoughte whiche indignacion sinfull woman hit wolde seme styring grete maulgry spared justifye woman yt demedno contra condione mala sinfull shewyng hir louyng god saued true bileue yt fayled therof withstodinge syde pharisee left fede hym hym humanite many men nowe done whiche time yt sothe sayd contrary opinion withdrawe humanite affeccion fro seyth neuer gode vertuous lyuinge sothely yt condicion shewe hem self euer ben vnlouing jhus sothfastnes vnkynde pharisee soo worthy reprefe peyne neuertheles ye prechouror nother ghostly man representeth cristes persone shall spare say ye soth time drede maulgre withdrawyng fauour ony temporel profite yf true membre crist soueraiuly ware glosing fauoure errour abhominable also processe said gospell yt lord jhus reherced pharisee gode dedes capitulum de sancto johanne baptista p spekynge oure lorde jhesu wyth woman samarytane atte pytte capitulum xxiii befelle vpon time lord jhus sholde go fro ye coutre juda galilee must make wey coutre samarye drawe welle called well jacob pitte water vpo whiche pytte rested hym wery goynge lord jhu thou yt arte sothfast wey maker erthly way soo arte wery wey whiche thorugh thy souereyne myght berest vp confortest way thus woldest thou thy manhede shewe thy kyndely infirmite man honger thurst werines oft sythes suche shewe kynde man thou tokest sake al thy bodily liuing worlde paynfull traueillous ensaple blessid thou euer mene time sat well disciple gone next cite bye men come woman coutre fette water yt welle ye whiche called lucy lord jhus willing shewe hyr hyr godhede spake hir long time grete thing hyghe innot ghostly vnd er stondyng whiche speking bothe hir disciple come ageyn woman worde peple cite come hym helde hem certeyne time went fro hem passen ouer time mykel hit open plainly wryten gospel john processe may note lord jhu first token grete mekenes wold alnota lone tyme sente disciple cite bey mete byenge ensample leefull goddes seruautes haue money reserue nede manere dedely syne assent moost perillous yf longe abyde specially yf ghostly hye pryde enuye saynt gregory sayth somtyme greuous syne goddes syghte pryde delyberacon herte dede lechery yet aldaye one gretly charged saye lechery seldom lityll therfore ben many men deceyued passe ouer reysynge seconde dede body wryten ye gospel saynt luke tyme lordeof dede bo jhus came cite named naym disciple wyth hym moche peple mette yate cyte dede body borne bere allone sone widow came wyth corse moche folke cytee wyth thene lorde hauynge pyte grete soro wydowe meued thrugh endles mercy badde yt sholde wepe thenne nighyng towchyng bere therwyth beren standinge styll spake body thyse wordes thou yonge man saye aryse vp anone rose fro dethe lyfe wente fete began speke soo betoke moder alyue ye processe gospel forsayd lorde jhu moche thy mercy shewed synfull man whiche thou reysedest dede body borne towarde beryeng prayer made styrynge thyn endles godenes pyte soo thou reysest daye ghostly hem dede soule grete synes flesshly ghostly yeuyng thy grace oft time thou prayed sought ony deserte thrugh whiche synfull men styred repentauce forsakyng syne soo shryfte penauce doynge lawes holy chirche ben reysed ghostly lyf grace first dede syne performed dede yf soo synne openly knowen euyl ensample sclauder thenne nede open penaunce holy chirche hath ordeyned lord jhus yaue ensample open reysynge forsayd dede body ope ly borne dede bere wythout forth syght peple bvt princypall purpose speke reysynge iii dede body saye lazar foure dayes dede asmoche processe ben many fayre grete notable thynges therfore shall specyally gader entente make v ymagynacon present bodily conuersacon wyth lorde jhu dyscyples also wyth blessed deuout meyne saye martha mary lazar specyally beloued lorde jesu gospell wytnessith fyrste shall vnd er stonde haue mynde processe nexte chapyter vpon tyme whan lorde jhus walked temple saye place called salamons porche feste dedicacyon temple jewes camen aboute hym rauysshynge wulues wood dogges wyth grete yre grenynge vpon hym sayeng thise maner wordes longe wolt thou make v suspese dwere hertes thou arte thou cryste telle v openly sayden bi false malycyous entent ende yt yf openly knowleged criste saye enoynted kynge thene haue taken hym accused hym traytoure cezar emperour rome therfore lorde jhus knowyng fals ymagynacon tempred wysly ansuere inocent lambe amonge soo many trechours wulues sobyrly mekely sayd hem agayne speke ye leue werke doo name fader tho beren wytnes ouer whan sayd fader alone token vppe stone haue stoned hym blasphemer makynge hym self god ferd er whan lorde concluded partye reason auctorytees holy wrytt myght ayen say notwythstodyng resonable meke ansuere soo goodly wordes contynueden encreasen malyce asmoche tyme passyon yet comen yeue ensaple penauce yeuynge stede woodnesse withdrewe hym hondes wente wyth discyples beyonde jordan place john baptyzed fyrste aboute xviii myle fro jherusalem dwelled awhile wyth discyples tyme soone gospell telleth purpoos lazar broder martha mary sayde wexed sore sike anone two systers senden worde jesu forsayd place beyonde jordan sayenge hym manere loo lorde thou loueste lazar sore seke sayden noo asmoche thought suffised hym loued wyst meaned also perauenture knowing malyce jewes agaynst hym deth lityl wolde haue stoned hym durst calle hym hem comytted wyll thene jhesus sayd hem infirmyte dethe praysyng god goddis sone glorifyed therby gospel tellyth yt sayd thise wordes hem specifyeth sister senden tyme present grete waye fro hym sayd neuertheles may vnd er stonde processe ansuerde hem thyse wordes messager elles sayd discyples bothe moost lykely lorde coforte systers whan herde messager thise wordes jhesus sayd infirmyte dethe vnd er stondyng peraue ture hym brod er sholde deye bodily infirmyte discomforte hem whan dede beryed vnd er stondynge oure lorde meaned gloryous reysynge folowed trowynge thenne sholde haue falle neuertheles dyscomforte ye tyme torned comfort desired fyrst wolde haue hym preserued fro deth helyd infyrmyte oure lorde jhus thus fallyth oft tymes wyth hem god loueth ben trybulacion disease lorde god grauteth hem comfort aske desyren suffreth hem tyme dispeyre desyre whan wyll fulfylleth desyre better wolde firste torneth disco forte comfort wolde haue ymagined thoughte ferd er processe gospel oure lorde certifyed seke lazar ansuere sayd dwellled styll forsayd place two dayes af sayd discyples goo agayne jewery aferde worde sayden maister right jewes wolde haue stoned wolte thou goo agayn thyder thene jhus ansuerde agayn ben twelue houres daye sayth ben ye aferde supposyng jewes contynue malyce wete ye well oft tymes houres chaugen daye ofte mane herte purpoos varyeth chaungeth goostly meanynge thyse wordes saynt austyn expowneth lord vnderstondyng hymself daye twelue discyples twelue houres daye reprehended mysbileue vnresonable drede deth wyll wold yeue couseyle hym men god dyscyples mayster seruautes lorde feble seke hym souerayne leche wherfore maner blamyng hem lorde sayd hem manere sente ce twelue houres daye walkyth day offendeth erreth folowe ye yf ye woll erre wyll ye yeue couseyle sythen nede take counseyle therfore sythen soo daye houres kindly reason houres folowe daye daye houres folowe ye yf ye woll offende erre oure lord jhus knowyng spiryte lazar dede sayd hem lazare oure frende slepyth woll goo wake hym reyse hym fro slepe thene discyples vnderstondyng flesshly tho wordes kyndly slepe sayden syre yf slepe token yt shall hole saaf sykenesse comynly way kynde slepe seke men token hele folowyng jhus meaned deth soo maye see grete homelynes lorde wyth discyples maner bourdyng spake wyth declaring hem openly spake fyrst mystlysayd lazar dede gladde therby bileue maye encreced strengthed knowyng tyme dethe soo rather byleuynge goddis sone ferd er leuynge many wordes gospell takyng semyth notable edyficacon aft wha lorde jhus wyth disciple torned agayn toward bodily sittynge mary home sayd martha goyng tyme mette ihu felle fete sayd lorde yf thou haddest ben brother dede neuertheles wote well soo euer yu askest god god wolle yeue durste saye vtterly desyred inwardly sayeng thus reyse brod er fro dethe lyfe wist whether expedient brod er sholde reysed whether ihesus wyll therfor set wordes discretly manere meanyng lorde wote well thou mayst reyse hym therfore yf yu wylt shall done whether yu wylt co mytte thy dome presupcon thene said ihs yt brod er sholde ryse fro deth life general wordes might taken two maners proue bileue fynall resurreccon specifyeng whether wolde reyse hym ye tyme none therfore martha takyng part syker byleue sayd yt wyste well shold ryse generall resurreccon laste daye dome ferd er askynge lorde whether bileued sayd yt resurreccon lyf euerlastyng lyf byleueden sothfastly hym answerde fynally thus byleue thou art criste goddis sone art come world mane sauacon thene byddynge ihus wente home called mary suster scilence saye soft spekyng sayeng maister comen calleth hun anone rose vp went loo expresly also tokened ghostly longeth contemplatyf lyfe saye fyrste reste pee scylence softe speche low de cryenge stylle martha mette fyrste wyth hym wolde doo reysynge lazar vnto tyme mary comen thene whan comen fallen downe atte ihus fete wyth sore wepynge teeres sayd dide yf brod er dede lorde ihus seenge wepyng loued soo specyally also jewes wepyng ye comen yt tyme coforte mary wept also iii cause first loue mary specyally syster lazar also ton b shewe greuousyte syne custome ghostly dethe thrugh tokened lazar foure dayes dede beried thirde mysbileue hem whiche byleued myght haue kept hym fro deth myghte thene reyse hym lyfe agayne soo woll thene inwardly take hede beholde lorde ihus wepith sister wepe jewes wepe ye elacrime ason tellyth discyples wepe skylfully maye stired compassion wepynge leest inwardly herte namly synne custome harde ouercome ryse lorde ihus shewed ghostly vnd er stondynge grete diffyculte made wepyng maner trowbling hymself two tymes wroth grutching spiryte reysed lazar vnd er stode syne custome oft sayd yeuynge ensaple saynt austyn saythaug thou arte reyse lyfe soule ouerlayed stone dedely synne custome many ben sayth saynt austyn peple whiche ben ouerlayed wyth heuy burden wycked custome peraucture beren ben ouercome wyth lechery gloteny appostle ye peryssh ansuerynge sayeng maye leue custome lorde jhu reyse thise folke thou reysedest lazar thou arte sothly resurreccon vprisyng lyfe heuily stone wicked custome ouerlayeth men degree lered lewde seculers also religyous nyghe astates soo woll speken ayenst wycked customes shall know sothly experyence noo remedye jhu lorde jhu crye thise men hye voys yt saye shewe thy myyte teyse hem lyfe grace puttynge away heuy stone wycked custome thou reysedest lazar thi crye thy biddyng rose vp wente graue yet bouden hondes fete tyll losed vnbou den thy discyples thy byddynge grete wonder saynt augustyn sayth many men myghte goo graue wyth fete bouden moche wonder rose fro dethe lyfe foure dayes dede beryed wyth body stynkynge careyne tokenyth sayth saynt augustyn sothly tokenith whan thou doost grete syne bi contept thou arte ghostly dede yf thou contynuest customably therin thene arte thou dede beried whan yu forthinkest within forth shryuest knowlegest thy synne wythout fourth thenne distourbled vncouth de de come tolde hem wold morowe goo openly jhrlm thene soueraynly aferde prayden hym hertly mod er also namely wolde put hymselfe soo vtterly enmyes hondes sothly ferd er dethe jhus tame jherusalem vpon palmsonday caplm xxxvii sondaye erly vpon morow lorde jhesus dysposed hym sayd goo jherusalem new maner vncouthe wyse euer dyde fulfyll prophecye zacarye prophete sayd solempne cytee jherusalem sothly thou dydest thyn dedes enformacon en sample may see vnderstonde maner worldes worshippe takynge thou dispisest fully po pe vayne worldes worshyp hauyuge stede golden har ney curyous sadels bridels symple clothes hem yn helters whan people herde comynge cause grete myracle publisshed reysinge lazar weten ayenst hym receyueden kynge wyth ympnes songes grete joyes strewynge waye clothes braunches tree wyth joye lorde meaned sorow wepyng whan came nyghe cyte wepte therupon sayenge destrucci therof came sorowynge ghostly blind nesse shall vnderstonde holy wrytte makyth mynde lorde wepte notably thre tymes one tyme theprimo dethe lazar wretchydnes mankynde wherby neded deth fyrste syne nother tyme wepte thesecudo ghostly blyndenes vncunynge man tyme hem dwellen cyte jherusalem wolden knowe tyme gracyous visytacon therfor come cyte vtter distruccon thir de tyme wepte grete trespaas malyce man andtercio tyme passion hangyng crosse sawe passyon sufficyent redempcon men neuertheles toke effecte profyte reproued harde hertes obstynate doo pena unce woll forthynke amende hem synes wepinge spekith appostle poul whan sayth jhus tyme passyon wyth grete crye wepynge teres herde fader reuerence thyse thre wepyng tymes holy wrytte spekyth also holy chirchequart makith mynde wepte fourth tyme yt whan yonge chylde wepynge hyde fro deuilles mysterye jncarnacon beholde lorde jhus soo wepynge feynyngly effectuelly largely wyth sorowfull herte specyally dampnacon without ende destruccon tem porell hem cytee maye sothfastly trowe dere moder company seenge hym wepyng soo myght conteyne hem fro wepyng tyme nomore sholde sene losse soules th lord jesus rydynge asse hauynge stede prynces erles boron poore symple discyples aboute hym wyth moder deuoute wymen folowynge entred solempne cyte also peple doynge hym great worshyp sayd whiche comynge al cyte gretly styred soo went firste temple cast oute therof byars seller agaynst goddis lawes sayde xxxii chapiter stondin ge openly temple prechynge ansuerynge prynces pharysees daye tyll drewe towarde euen soo discyples stondyng daye fastynge grete worshyp done one wolde bydde hym one drynke subtill temptynges soo occupied fro morowe vnto euentyde whan went wyth discyples rest homly hostrye wyth lazar systers bethanye sayd asmoche longe processe trete specyall tho mater tyme bytwene lorde jhus jewes lettynge fro ye purpoos passyon therfore passinge ouer parable ensamples whiche lorde repreheded jewes processe tyme spe syall maye generall consyder note yt one syde prynces pharisee worthy dethe lorde preuyte mannes herte open knowyng subtylte malyce hem ansuerde wysely questyons soo couertly trou sette wordes sufficyetly answerde yet myghten haue entent ony part laste confouded durst nomore aske oni questyon hym thenne lorde jhus sharply reprehended pride ypocrysy couetyse wyckyd condycons hem specyally scrybes pharisee sa yenge hem thise wordes woo scrybes pharisee louen worldly worshippes many maners soo fourth vyces neuertheles badde therwyth peple sholde kepe fulfyll techynges sholde folowe werkes euyll liuyng last rehersynge vnkyndnesse jewes ayest god generall borde john next jhu vpon grou de maner olde men shall vnderstonde boorde square men supposen made dyuerse boordes joyned togyder men sayen hane seen rome chyrche latranensis conteyneth euery parte ye foure square space two armes lengthe somwhat soo euery syde square borde dyscyples saten men supposen though streyghtly lorde jhus angle soo myghte reche myddes ete one dysshe therfore vndstode hym tyme sayd wyth puttith honde dysshe dobler shalle bitraye thus may ymagyne suppose mane sittynge borde also maye vndstonde etynge paske lambe tyme stoden abouteagn pa schal borde vpright holdinge staues hondes bid dynge moyses lawe lorde came fulfylle soo though stoden tyme neuertheles seten also tyme gospell tellith dyuers place elles myght john haue layed hede rested hym manere lyggynge vpon breste jhu tyme paske la broughte boorde rosted lawe lordagn pa sc al jhus sothfast lambe god wythout weme synne myddes hem seruith minystreth toke lambe blessyd hodes cutte departed yaaf discyples byddyng hem ete glad ly comfortyng hem wyth louely chere though eten badde neuertheles cofort myght thei none haue asmoche dradde alwaye leest sholde falle ought ayenst lorde nouelte eten tolde hem sorowfull dede openly sayd haue desired ete wyth paske labe suffre deth sothly one shal bytraye speche wente hertes sharpe swerde wherfore essed etynge loked eche sayden hym lorde whether yf take good hede owen haue inwarde copassion bothe lorde jhu also hem noo doubte full grete sorowe tray tour juda lefte etynge thise wordes bitrayeng sholde seme perteynyng hym thene john instauce peter asked lorde sayd lorde shall bytraye lorde jhus pryuely tolde hym hym loued specyally specifyed traytour john therof gretly astonyed wodred wyth grete sorowe herte nought wolde telle peter torned hym jhu softely layed downe hede vpo blessyd breste saynt augustyne sayth oure lorde jhesu wolde telle peter traytoure hadaug omelia di je petro wyste wolde haue torne hym wyth teeth saynt augustyn sayth peter ben fygured vnderstode ben actyff lyfe john ben con templatyff wherfore haue doctryne fygure cotemplatyff medlith hym wyth foreyne worldly dedes also sechith vengaunce wythout forth offeses done god sory wythin forth herte torneth hym god deuout prayer sadly tornynge hym drawynge hym god commyttith thynge disposycon ordenaunce though soo cotemplatyff sotyme gooth zele god profyte mannes soules whan called therto also john wolde telle peter badde hym aske traytour maye vnderstonde comtem platyf shall reuele secrete lorde wrytenn de sco frac saynt fransoys preuy reuelacons reueled outforth tyme nede made hym hele ne soules stirynge god reuelacon meued forth processe beholde grete benygnyte lorde jhu soo homly suffred der ynge john enclyne reste vpon blessed breste lorde tend er ly truly loued togyder swete rest john profytable crysten soules whiche clerkes sayen dronke welle euerlastynge wysdome precyous drynke holy gospell wyth whiche comfor ted al holy chirche yaaf triacle ayenst venym diuers heretikes beholde ferd er discyples full sory forsayd worde bitrayenge lord jhu et nge lokynge eche wyste counceyle comforte myght haue caas thus moche tyme suffysith touchinge fyrst artycle yt bodily supper etyng paske lambe fulfyllyng lawe endynge fygure oure lorde jhus dyde fore clerkes sayen fynde lorde ete flesshe lyfe oonly tyme etyng la mystery bodily fode towchynge thes pedu abl seconde poynte wasshyng discyples fete shall vnd er stonde forsayd processe lord jhus rose vp fro supper also discyples anone wyth hymb vnwitynge wold doo ferd er whether wolde goo thene
