herde threte nynge elles sholde haue noo parte wyth blysse torned wyll better mekely suffred yf yeue gode entent dedes lord jesu folowyth tyme sothly maye grete wonder styred specyally loue drede hym see kynge blysse hygh lorde mageste knele downe bowe hym fete poore fysshar soo forth seten soo wyth blessed hondes wysshe foule fete tendlynotahumilitat wyped hem ouer deuoutly kyssed hem soothly yt souerayne maister mekenes shewed v dede taughte v perfyte lesson therof yet morouer yt dyde lowe seruyce traytour comeuded soueraynly passynge mekenes wo harde herte ye harder adamaunt ony thynge hardest melteth softeth wyth hete soo grete fyre charyte profoude mekenesse dredeth lorde mageste dede ay warde frowardly thynkyth procureth dethe destruccon hym euer soo inocent soo true louynge wherfore bothe wond er dredful grete benygnyte mekenesse lorde jhu grete obstynacy malyce traytoure juda ayenwarde whan wasshynge done mystery sayd wente agayne vp place forsayd supper whan sette wyth theym tolde theym cause forsayd dede sholde folowe hym mekenesse eche gaaf hem ensample theyr lorde maister shold wasshe others fete also foryeue trespaces done wyll doo good vnd er stonde wordes folowen whan said hem ye knowen thise haue done ye shall blessed yf ye fulfylle hem dede also fyrste messe paske lambe sayde whan wasshen made clene serued wyth seconde messe precyons body deynte deyntes men vsen bodily fedyng festes f ste serued wyth boystous homly mete delycate deynteous wherof folowyth herafter wchynge thirde artycle anenst thyrde artycle hy est sacrament jhesus precyous body lyfte bertes soueraynly bethynke inwardly wondrynge ye moost worthy dygnacyon vnspeable charyte thrugh whiche betoke hymselfe v lefte v e ghostly foode makynge ordeynynge precyous sacramente manere whan wasshen discyples fete goone vp agayne wyth hem sate supper sayd ende sa fyces olde lawe begynnynge newe testamet makyng hymself sacrefyce toke brede holy hondes lyft vp eyen fader almyghty god blessed brede sayd wordes consecracon therouer vertue whiche wordes brede torned body thenne yaaf discyples sayd taketh eteth sothly body shall take yeue manere takynge chalyce wyth wyne sayd takith drynkith alle herof blode yt shall shedde many redempcyon synes yaaf power ye consecracon prestes hem sayd thus dooth ye oft ye take comemoracon mynde take gode thou crysten man specyally thou preste deuoutly dy ligently truely thy lorde jhus cryste made fyrste precyo sacrament wyth blessed hondes minystred commyned blessed byloued meyne syde take hede wyth deuoute wond er fyrste sawe hym make wonderfull excellent sacrament drede reuerece toke receyued hym sothly tyme lefte kyndly reason man rested true byleue sayd dyde byleue wythoute ony doubte god myghte erre soo must thou doo wolte fele haue vertu ghostly swetnesse blissed sacrament thisb swete precyous memoryale soueraynly makith man soule worthy plesynge god ofte duely receyued eyther true deuoute meditacon passion elles specyally sacramentale etynge therof wherfore reson excellent yeft loue shold kyndle mane soule enflame holy yeuer therof oure lorde jhus cryste noo thynge myght yeue leue v derworth swete profy table hymself without ony doubte receiuen sacrament aulter self goddis sone jhesus toke flesshe blode borne vyrgyn mary suffred deth crosse v rose thirde daye fro dethe lyfe styed vp heuen sittyth faders ryght side shall come daye dome deme makynde whoos power bo lyfe dethe made bothe heuen helle onli maye saue v dapne v euer wythout ende soo self god man conteyned lityll oost thou seest forme brede eueri daye offred vp fader ofn heue ghostly hele euerlastyng sauacon true bileue holy chirche hath tauyte v blessid sacrament yet ouer lete v sitte lityll loger worthy lordes boorde jhus take hede inwardly oure ghostly foode comforte specyally precyous moost de teous mete sette v blessed body lorde jhus holy sacramet beforsayd inwarde cosideracon taaste swetnesse heuenly fode hauynge fyrst mynde gracious resonable makyng ordenauce blessed sacramet ye grete worthines merueylous werkyng therof chosen soules coforte strengthyng fayth anenst ye firste poynt shall vnd er stonde almyghty euerlastyngly yaaf al cristen people body mete blode drynke vnd er lyknesse brede wyne manere sayd fyrst makyng blessed sacrament beholde inwardly take hede wondrynge appostles thenne see oure lorde jhus man syttynge wyth hem bodily therwith holdyng hondes self body semyd bodi syghte noughte elles brede affermynge thus sothly body shall yeuen also chalyce semed oonly wyne bloode shall shedde remyssion synnes soo self bodi sene wyth bodily eyen hem sothly vnd er forme brede self blode hole bodi chalice forme wyne thenne brede semid wordes co secracon wyne semid self maner liknes fourme brede wyne conteynynge crystes flesshe blode sayd mane wytte reason myghte comprehende att tyme sothly none therfore true apostle tyme leften bodily reason wytte rested true byleue lordes wor de sayd befor sauf juda reproued falshede mysbyleue therfore receyued blessed sacotra lol lardos crament dampnacon done tho parte whiche falsly bileuen sayen holi sacramente aulter kynde brede wyne consecracon cause semyth soo bodily felynge syght taast touchyng whiche reprouable parte juda sene jhus bodily beside sacrament dyde therfor lyghter hem byleue dampnacion yf byleue god holy chirche hath taughte namly sythen true techinge blessed sacramente hath holden stedfastly soo many hudred yeres sofides sacrameti many holy men marters confessours true cristen men whiche laste dayes stoden without doubte faythe deyden therin whiche fewe wordes sacrament aulter duely made vertue crystes wordes goddis body forme brede blode forme wyne though forme brede wyne seme alle bodily wyttes man brede wyne kynde neuertheles soo othnes oonli goddis flesshe blode substaunce accydents brede wyne wonderfully myraculously agaynst mane reason comyn order kynde holy sacrament wyth kyndly subiect cristes body suffred deth vpo crosse sacrament bodily vnder forme lyknesse brede blood vnder lyknes wyne substancyally holy wythout ony feynyng deceyte oonly fygure asnot fals heretyke sayth thise termes touche soo specially cause lewde lollardes medlen hem agaynst fayth falsly ouer sayd fayth holy chirche touchynge excellent sacrament taughte holy doctours worthy clerkes confermed many maneres shall sare ouer somwhat specyall knowe sothly gracyous werchynge sensible felinge blessid sacramente whiche merueylously werching felyngeaboue comin kynde man shewyth proueth soueraynly blessed body presence jhu sacrament one persone know liuynge perauenture ben many know selfe degree hygher whiche persone tymes whan lord jhesus vouchesauf touche hym grace tretynge blessed sacrament wyth inwarde siyght soule deuout meditacon presious passion sodeynly felyth also shedde body joye likynge passyth wythout comparyson hyghest likynge ony creature may haue fele way kynde lyfe thrugh whiche joye likynge membres bodi enflamed soo delectable joyefull hete hym thynkyth sensibly alle body meltynge joye waxe dooth anenst hote fyre ferforth ye body might bere excellent likyng shold vtterly faylle nere gracyous kepynge susteynyng towcher lorde jhu aboue kynde lorde jhu delectable paradise tyme thus felith blessid bodily presence precions sacrament thrugh ye whiche felyth hym sensybly wyth vnspeable joye joyned body body sothly trowe yt maye man telle speke syker maye noo man fully sothfastly knowe experyence felyth wythoute doubte specyally hydde mana saye angel mete man knowyth felyth saynt john witnessith apolipse yt soothfastly felyth maye well saye wyth dauyd prophete soueraynly reioycynge body soule herte flesshe god alyue lorde jhesu moche multytude thy swetnessequam magna multitu dulce dinis thou hast hydde hem true loue dreden thus haue vnd er stonde forsayd gracyous wond er full myraculous worchinge lorde jhu shewynge sensibly blessyd delectable bodily presence moost thornes whiche perced greuously brayne pane made ful blode soo scorned hym yf wolde haue regned yt myght al suffreth sernaute knaue wretch dredful shal yt hede appere last whiche ye smyten boldli yet suffiseth malice mo reproue scorne hem gadred al wicked copany fyrst wonder vpon hym hous broughte hym pylate al peple maner illuded ye crowne thornes yt olde purpur vestyment see goddis loue stant maner haging face dou ne towarde erthe grete multytude cryenge askynge pylate crucifye crucyfie hym scorning hym wold make hym wyser prynces pharysees doctours law wysdom torneth grete foly shewed tyme soo suffred grete paynes sorow body wythin also many foule abredgynges reproues wythoute forth p lorde jhus dapned dethe crosse aboute tyerce daye caplm xlii lord jhus longe tyme tormented illuded sayd prynces jewes wyth grete instaunce contynuelly askeden maden ye multytude wyth hem crye aske sholde crucyfyed last wretched justyce pylate dredynge offende hem condempne innocent wrongefully yaaf sentence vpon hym wyll soo dampned hym hanged crosse thene prynces pharysees ald er men joyefull gladde entent fulfylled haue mynde grete benefyces wond er full dedes hath shewed hem also moued pite innocence cruel hem ben slaked withdrawen fro malyce grete despytes paynes haue seen done hym laughen maken joye scornen hym god maye dampne hem euerlastynge dethe soo besien hem maye bryng hym hastely dethe wherfore ladde agayn hous scorged illuded draw fro hym olde purpyll mantell soo alle naked beden clothe hymself ayen wyth inwarde copasson beholde hym manere sayd oonly manhede passyng soo fayre yonge man moost innocent moost louely maner rente wounded blody naked wyth maner shamefastnes gadryng hys clothes dyuerse place hous dysclatered thoo harlottes doynge hem honest maner hem euer lowghen hym scorne though thenota de paciec tada moost wretche al forsaken god wythoute al maner socoure helpe p wherfore nowe take hede dyligently hym haue wounder grete profounde mekenes hym moche thou mayste conforme folowe hym pacyence mekenes suffrynge wronge loue gooth forth wyth beholde hath done clothes ladden hym forth grete haste layne vpon hym worshipful tree crosse heuy full long saye wryten storyes xv foote lengthe ye whiche meke moste pacient lambe toke vpon sholders bereth forth soo ladde forth wyth twoo felawes theues dampned self dethe felawship tyme good lord jhu shame done yt sholde frendes maken felawe theues yet done worse maken bere youre crosse redde hem wherfore oonly prophete ysaye sayth ye putte wyth wicked doer theues also wythcu ini deputatus est worse theues sothely lord thy pacience may spoken p ferthermore processe seenge dere moder myghte folowe nyghe grete multitude peple aboute toke another waye short haste johan felawship yt myyte mete wyth hym waye whan mette wyth wythoute yate cyte ii wayes metten gyder sawe charged ouerlayd wyth soo grete tree ye crosse ye whiche sawe halfe dede sorowe soo neyther myghte speke hym one worde hir cause grete haast hem ladden hym jewes lityl lorde torned hym wymen folowed hymfilie iherlm nolite sle super wepyng sayd hem ye doughters jhrlm wepith forth gospell thise ii place made chirches mynde thise thiges sayen haue seen hem ferthermore cause mount caluarie crucyfied grete space fro yate cyte atter ouer come wyth traueyle wery myghte noo lenger bere heuy crosse layed doune cursed tormentours full malyce dredynge dyfferre deth leest pylate wold haue called ayen sentence dome shewed befor wyll haue delyuerde hym maden nother man called symon bere crosse ladden hym soo discharged crosse bouden bondes behynde hym theif place jewesse mount caluarye yf yu take good hede hath done lorde jhu yt suffred matyn tyme pryme tyerce tyme shall seen matere grete copassion grete passion sorowe sothly ib trowe yes namly yf thou wolt make thy mynde recapitulacon reherce generall hath suffred hath done tyme thynken yt lorde jhus god blessed aboue thynges fro hour taken nyghte tyme hys crucyfienge cotynuel batayle grete reproues despytes sorowes illusion tormentes yeue himn hic valde bene cessu hora mat na rest euer traueylle paynes sorowes yf yu wolte knowe coflyct batayle beholde see fyrst one dispytously layth hode hym takyth nother redy harde byndeth hym nother cryenge puttyth hym blaspheme another spytteth hys face another sothely asketh hym many questyons deceyte accuse hym another besy brynge fals witnesse agaynst hym another draweth forth iustice another styfly accuseth another hydeth eyen another buffeteth hym anotherhora prima despoyleth another byndeth hard pyler another wyth sharpe scourge beteth another vnbyndeth hym casteth hym olde silken mantell another setteth croune sharp thornes hede another putteth hond de another taketh wodely fro hym smyteth sore hede ful thornes another kneleth forth one another diuerse many witte myyte syen hem tormente hym worst maner leden hym theef byshop anne cayphas pylate herode hederward thederward lord god al loo thyn keth full hard continuell bytter trauayle yet abyde lytyll whyle thou shalt see harder standen styfly agaynst hym allone prynces pharysees scrybes thousandes people cryeng one voys crucifyed last iustice pylate yeueth dome crucyfied anone heuy crosse layd sholders rente broken woundes hys scourgyng ferthermore beholde thy lord goyng forthe wyth crosse back thene oute cyte yates rennen bothe cyteyzens straungers al degree oonly gentyles also foulest rybaudes wyndryn kers haue compassion woder vpon scorne none wyl knowe pyte uous affeccion rather fylth vnclennesse al despisen reprouen prophete sayth parabole mouthes soo seten yates iuges speken agaynst hym tho dronken wyne lust maden songe hym th drawen hasted grete vyolence wythout reste tyll cam foule stynkyng place caluarye sette ende reste harde batayle speke maner reste wherof shall treate sothly harde tree deth sharper batayle lo reste certaynly bedde soro thus mayst thou see generall contemplacon harde batayle thy lord hath suffred sexte houre wherof shall treate folowynge processe blessed pas p crucifyenge lorde jhhesu sexte houre caplm xliu ferdermore mayste thou see whan lorde jhesus come stynkynge hylle caluarie wyckedly tho cursed werke began werche alle sydes cruell werke take hede dylygently wyth thy herte tho thynges ben come make preset thy myude beholdinge shall done agaynst thy lord jhu ben spoken done soo juner eye thi soule beholde sittynge fytchynge crosse faste erthe makynge redy nayles hamers dryue hem wyth makynge redy settynge vp ladder deynynge instrumentes hem thought nedfull faste spoyle hym drawe clothes soo thyrde tyme spoyled stondeth naked syghte peple soo ben thyrde tyme nued brysours woudes scorgrnge cleuynge clothes flesshe also fyrst moder seeth taken ordeyned deth wherfore sorouful mesure hauyng shame see hym sto dynge naked left somoche pryue clothes went haste dere sone clypped hym gyr de hym aboute lendes wyth kircheif hede lorde sorowe soule whan seeth suche despite done sone sothly trowe myght speke one worde sorowe might doo nomor hym helpe hym yf myght wythout doubte wold thene sone anone taken handes wood maner ladde fote crosse take hede dilygently maner crucifyeng ben set vp ii ladder one behinde another last terme crosse whiche ii wicked minysters gone vp wyth nayles hamers also another short ladder sette crosse la steth vp place fete sholde nayled take good hede al folowyth lorde thene copel led beden goo vpo ladder crosse kely dooth beden whan came ouerest ende short ladder torned backe crosse stretched brode ii kinges armes fairest ha de yaaf hem crucifyed hym thenne lyftynge vp eyen heuen sayd fader thise maner wordes lonota verba filii ad prem dere fader thou woldest sholde loowe vnto crosse sauacon makynde pleysynge acceptable hem offre myselfe whiche thou woldest sholde bretherne wherfore also thou fader take gladly sacrifyce hem hen forwarde pleysed well wylled hem loue olde offence trespace foryeue wype awaw put aferre vnclenes syne fro hem sothly offre theim hele thenne ladder behynde crosse takyth ryghte honde ladder behynde crosse taketh hys ryght honde nayleth fast crosse lifte syde draweth whyth myghte lyttt arme honde dryueth ther thruy another grete nayle comen doune taken aweye ladder hangeth lorde oonely tho two nayles smyten thrugh hondes wythoute sustenaunce body drawynge dounwarde peynfully thorugh weyght therof wyth also another harlot renneth draweth doune fete wyth myghte another anone dryueth grete longe nayle thorugh bothe fete joyned one maner hys crucifyenge oppynyon men ther ben trowen crucyfyed maner fyrste lyggynge crosse ground nayled hym therupon wyth hym hangyng lyften vp crosse festen doune erthe yf done maner thenne mayst thou see hou vylaynsly taken hym rybaulde casten hym doune vpon crosse thene wode theues drewen bothe sydees fyrst hys hondes hys fete soo nayled hym fast crosse wyth myghte lyften vp crosse wyth hangyng hyghe myghte thene lete falle dooune moiteyse whyche falle thou mayst vnd er stonde senowes breken hys souerayne payne whether soo hit one maner sothe lord jhus nayledbn hard vpon crosse honde foote soo streyned drawen hym self sayth prophete dauyd thatdinue tauerut os mea myghte telle nombre hys bone thene rennen oute hys blessyd body stremes holyest blood sydes habondauntly fro grete woundes soo con streyned arted maye meue hys hede wherfore hangynge body onely tho thre nayles noo doubte suffreth bytter sorowe paynes maye noo herte thynke ne tonge telle yet ouer hanged bytwene two theues whiche one blasphe myed tepted hym jnpacyece therwith blasphe myng scornynge sayen vath destroyeth temple god makith vp ayen iii dayes sayde made sauf maye saue hymself many reproues scornynges sayden hym gospel tellyth thise reproues blasphemyes despite ben done seenge herynge moost soroufull moder whosenotabn copassion sorowe made hym sone haue bytter payne half henge soule sone crosse desyred inwardly rather haue deyed tyme wyth hym haue lyued lenger soo stode moder besyde crosse sone bytwene crosse crosse theif torned neuer eyen fro full anguyssh also prayed fader tyme wyth herte sayenge thus fader andn ne filio god wythout ende pleysyng sone shol de crucifyed done yet tyme aske hym ayen ye see anguyssh soule beseche ye woll ease paynes good fad er recommende maye dere sone also sone prayed pryuely hymself sayenge fader yen ne filii mre knowe moder tormented sholde crucifyed loo hangeth crosse wyth myn owne crucifyenge suffyseth bere synes peple hath deserued ony suche thing wherfor recomende ye make paynes lesse thene lady john mawdleyn biloued discyples freudes crosse lorde jhu whiche maden grete sorow wepten myghte comforted noo maner byloued mayster euer sorow renewed wyth sorow eyther reproues dede foloweth p lord jhus yelded vp spiryte none xliiii hangeth oure lorde jhesus crosse grete payne yet ydle cause payn wroughte alwaye spake profytable v wherfo son v ba hangynge spake vii table wordes ben fouden writen gospell first tune crucifyed hym wha prayed hem sayengep vb pt igno illis dm mul e e filius tu te c hodieme cu eris paradiso quartu hely hely lama zabatani thus fader foryeue hem wite nought thei done whiche worde worde grete pacience grete loue vnspeka ble benygnyte secode moder sayeng th woman loo thy sone also john loo thy moder called time moder leest sholde thrugh feruent tend er ne haue ben sory thyrde blessed theyf sayenge daye thou shalt wyth paradise wherin moost large merci openly shewed fourth whan sayd hely hely lamazabatany saye god whi hast yu forsake though said sentece god fad er heuen yu hast somoche loued redempcon worlde thou hast yeuen therfore semed forsaken lo jhu coforte forsayd worde thyn enmyes discoforte thy frendes sothly semyth neuer worde oure lorde spake yaaf moche boldenes hys enemyes moche occasion hys frendes despayre god worde vnderstode hit tyme nakedly theletter souneth lord wold shewe last ende suffred body fully kynde man also hisb n spekynge infirmyte man man suspendyng tyme vse myghte ye godhe de v worde sicio thursty whiche wordequintu scicio also occasion moder johan frendes grete compassiou wicked enemyes grete reioicing gladnes though soo may vnd er stonde worde sicio thyrst ghoostly entent thyrsted thene ye hele soules neuertheles also sothnes thirsted bodily cause grete passing oute blood thrugh al drye withinforthe thyrsty thene tho wycked deuils lymes yt euer cast hou myght moost noye token eysell gall profered vp drinke cursid wo denes hem yt ben neuer filled wyth malyce al tymese tu consu matu est noyen moche mowen sexte word sayd cosumatu est al ended though sayde thus fader obedience thou hast yeuen haue par fytely fully done dede yet redy doo soo thou bydde wryten fulfylled wherfore yf thy wyll call ageyn thene sayde fader come swete loued sone thou hast done well thynges wyll thou tormented therfore come shall clyppe withnota de modo moriedi myn armes take tn bosome tyme lord began fayle syghte maner deynge men waxe plae stynkyng eyen openyng bowed hede one syde another side fayllingsepti mnm verbu pater man strengthes veynes thene voyde atte last put seuenth worde wyth stronge crye wepynge teres sayenge thus fader comende spiryte thy hondes therwith yelded vp spirite bowyng hede vp brest towarde fader maner thankyng called hym yeuynge hym spiryte crye thene couerted centurio beyng sayd sothly thisvere filius de tat ste man goddis sone cause sawe soo cryeng deye men whan deye maye crye herfore byleued sothly crye grete holy sayen herde helle lorde god hat state tyme mod er soule whan sawe hym pa fully fayle wepe deye sothly trowe e mul tytude anguysshes oute vn iable made half dede moche tyme mette wyth hym beryng crosse sayd trowe dyde thene mawdlayne true loued discyplesse john owne derlynge systers lady myghte doo ful sorow byt ternesse therfore wepten sore wythout remedye lo hanged lorde crosse dede grete multytude gooth awaye towarde cyte soroufull mod er wyth iiii systers felawes sette doune besyde crosse beholdeth pyteously dere sone soo ferde wyth abideth helpe fro god myght haue hym bene hym thene also yf thou beholde well thy lorde thou mayste haue matere ynough hyghe copassyon seenge hym tormented fro sole fote highest parte hede noo hole place ne mebre wythout passion pyteous syght joyeful syghte pyteous sighte hym harde passion suffred sauacon likynge syghte v matere theffecte haue therby redempcon sothly sighte lorde hangynge soo crosse deuout ymagynacyon soule soo lykynge somme creature longe exercyse sorowfull compassion felen somtyme soo grete lykyng soule also body telle maye noo man knowe alonly experyence felyth thenne may hemichi aute absit glori ari well saye wyth appostle betyde neuer joyefull crosse lorde jhu cryste amen p tho thynges befell deth lorde jhu none eplm xlv time worshipful moder lord jhesuca xlv b n sayd next abode dwellyd besyde ye crosse wyth true louers hym named beholdynge lord jhesu contynuelly pytously hangynge dede crosse betwene two theues lo thene come many armed men oute cyte toward hem whyche sente breke legges hem crucyfyed slee hem alle oute burye hem cause bodyes shold abide hangynge crosse sabotte day thene rose vp lady alle wyth hyr besyly loked sawe hem come wote wherfore falle grete sorowe drede namely lady spekynge hir sone thys maner dere sone maye cause al armed men comen agayene wyl doo haue slayne dere sone hadde hoped ben fylled wyth haue done semeth yet pursuen dede wote maye doo maye helpe myghte delyuer fro dethe shal abide see praye thy fader make hem softe easy ther wyth alle fyue yeden stoden byfore crosse oure lorde thene come forsayd armed men hem grete wodenes noyse seenge theues yet lyuyng wyth grete ire hewen breken despytously legges slewe hem caste hem anone diche besyde torned hem agayne camen towarde oure lorde jhu wherfore lady dredynge leest wolde doo maner sone thrugh smyten wyth sorowe herte within forth cowde nought elles goo beste armure saye kyndly mekenesse knelyng doune hem spredyng hodes wyth hygh voys wepyng chere spake hem maner good bred er n beseche almyghty goddis loue ye torment nomore dere sone sothly sorouful moder ye knowe wel brethern neuer offended dyde ony wronge though soo sone semed contraryous ye haue slayne hym foryeue wronge offence ye dethe sone wherfore dooth mercy ye breke ye haue done theues soo maye berye body hole nedith sythen ye seen fully dede longe tyme passed therwyth john magdalene systers knelynge wyth lady besoughten wyth sore wepynge lady doo ye ye lowen fete hem ben moost wycked prayen hem haue noo rewarde ony good prayer suppose ye bowe pyte hem ben moost cruell moost wycked wythout pyte ouercome hem ben alder proudest mekenes naye proude men haue abhomynacon mekenes ye traueyllen vayne therwyth one named longius tyme wycked proude true lyuer marter despisyng wepyng prayer wyth sharpe spere openyd syde oure lorde jhesu made grete wounde whiche anone rane togyd er bothe bloode water therwyth lady felle doune swounyug half dede bytwene harmes magdalene john mowynge bere grete sorow toke hym mane hert risyng ayenst hem sayd ye wycked doo ye cruelte see ye dede woll ye also slaye woman moder go way shall berye hym therwyth god wolde wente waye thene lady excyted rose fro slepe askynge done sone sayd none newe thynge ayenst hym caughte spiryte behelde sone soo greuously wounded also wouded herte wyth newe woude sorow seest thou oft time lady day dede sothly oft sawe done ayest sone oni payne wherfore fulfylled symeon sayd prophecyengt ipsi ptrasibit glad longe suerde shal perce thrugh thyn oune soule saye suerde passon sorowe befelle oft tymes daye sothly suerde spere hath perced body sone soule mod er saten doune besyde crosse shall doo wote may take un body berye cause haue neyther stregthe instrumentes apte therfore goo awaye fro hym soo hangynge dare longe abyde may cause nyghte come hem mayst thou see sorow perplexyte ben benygne lorde jhesu ye suffre dere moder chosen myrrour worlde youre specyall restynge place soo tormeted troubled vnneth hathe ony spiryte lyue tyme manere reste relecynge sorowe p takynge doune crosse lordes body jhesu euensonge tyme caplm xlvi mene tyme oure lady johan sayd soo grete perplexyte desolacion sayd lokeden toward cyte oftymes dyden drede thenne see many comynge towarde hem waye whyche joseph armathre nycodeme bryngynge wyth hem dyuerse instrumentes wyth whyche sholde take doune body jhu fro crosse also broughte hondred pou de myrre aloe anoynte body soo burye hyt thene rysen vp wyth grete drede knowynge wold lord god grete thy sorowe daye thene johan taking hede hem coming sayd lady sothely see comyng joseph nichodeme thene lady caughte spiryte gretely comforted sayd blessed oure lord god hath sente v helpe oure nede hath mynde oure sorowe hath forsake v oure trybulacyon good sone johan goo agaynst hem welcome hem wote well come socoure anone johan wente agaynste hem metten clipped wyth wepynge teres myghte speke grete whyle tendernes co passyon sorowe hadde walked forth lytyll whyle drawen nyghe towarde crosse joseph asked wythe lady stode wyth ye dyscyples johan answerynge tolde hem whoo wyth lady discyples coude tell sayd none hem sene day ferthermore askynge tolde done agaynst lord processe passyon come nygh place knelynge doune wepynge honoured lorde jhesu metynge togyder lady systers mawdleyne receyued hem worshipfully knelyng low bowynge therthe ayen warde knelynge worship pynge wyth grete wepynge stoden soo togyder grete whyle speken last lady began speke hem said sothly frendes ye hane done wel ye haue mynde mayster loued well knowlege plainly semyd newe light rysen comynge wyste myighte doo therfore god quyte sayden ayewarde ben sory wyth herte thyse wronges malice done ayenst hym seen well wycked men hauen maystry ayenst ryghtwysman wolde full gladly haue delyuerde fro grete jniury yf mighte leest shal seruyce lorde maister ben come fore thene made hem redy take hym downe take good hede maner haue sayd maner takynge downe sette ii laders sydes crosse one ayenst another joseph gooth vpon ladder stodynge yt houde right halfe besteth hym drawe nayle yt honde full harde nayle grete longe harde driuen ye tree wythout grete thirstyng doune lordes hode may done noo force lorde knowyth doyth al truly good entent therfore acceptith dede whan nayle drawen iohn makith sygne nychode take hym priuely soo lady see dyscomfortynge manere nychodeme drawyth oute nayle lyfte honde takyth pryuely johan thenne nychodeme comyth doune draw thirde nayle fete meane tyme joseph susteyneth body soothly well hym maye susteyne clyppe holyest body lorde jhesu therwyth lady takyth hondes reuerently oure lordes ryght hode beholdeth layeth eyen deuoutly kissith sore wepyng sighinge wha nayle fete drawe joseph came softly al layden honde token lordes body layed doune vpon therthe lady toke ye hede sholders layed arme mawdaleyn redy take kisse fete ye whiche foude somoche grace lyf copany stoden aboute beholding al makyng grete lamentacon vpo hym prophecye yt thene fulfylled sayeng yt thei shold make sorowe vpon hym vpon one begeten chylde namly blessed mod er al tymes sore wepyng soroufuly beholdynge woudes hondes fete specyally ye horryble woude syde takynge hede one another seege hede foule ferde wyth bere drawe wyth ye sharpe thornes louely face defouled wyth spittynges blode here berde drawen awaye fro chekes prophete ysaye spekyth persone th yaaf blode hem smytten chekes hem drewen awaye p beryenge lorde jhesu complyn tyme caplm xlvii lityll whyle lyenge body lorde jhesu bytwene moders armes sayde whan drewe towarde nyghte joseph prayed lady wolde suffre body dressed manere jewes beryed looth therto sayd good bredern take soo soone childe fro rather berieth wyth thene sayd john dere moder lete v assent joseph nychomede suffre oure lordes body beryed elles occasyon tomoche taryenge ye myght falle lyghtly dangeour sclauder ye jewes att suggestyon john lady wyse discrete thynkynge yt comytted lorde wolde noo lenger lette beryenge blessed body lete hem dresse wolde john nichodeme joseph began enoynt body wrappe lynnen clothe manere jewes beryenge neth eles lady kept alwaye hede lappe dresse herselfe mawdleyne fete wha dressed legges camen nygh ye fete mawdleyne sayd praye suffre dresse fete whiche fonde somoche grace suffryng askyng helde fete loked vpon hem weping almost fayling sorowe right lyf wyssh wyth teres copunccon moche wasshyth wyth teeres grete sorowe inwarde copassion sothfastnesse witnessith moche loued therfore wept moche namly last seruice doyng mayster lorde soo deed piteously vnethes sorow myight herte abyde body wold ful gladly haue deyed lordes fete sawe neuer remedye besieth wyth al might ye last seruice hym ye whiche ful vncouth dresse body best maner yt may wold hath neyther matere wherof tyme therto netheles maner maye wasshith fete teres deuoutly wypeth hem kysseth hem wrappeth clothes best maner whan haue done dressed body hede loken lady yt wolde performe parte thene began al mekely wepe make sorowe thenne seenge may noo lenger differ sett th sight vpo ye face sone spekith hym maner swete sone holde dede mi lappe see must depart bodili harde ye departyng dede befor likyng couersacon bitwene v liuynge amoge men euer wythout playnt offence though soo thou arte slayne wycked man haue serued ye truely thou sorouful batayle thy fad er wolde helpe myghte wherfor yu forsoke thyself loue mankynde thou woldest ayenbye ful harde painful dere bienge wherfore neuertheles gladde hele sauacon men thy passion deth full harde torme ted wote wel thou dydest neuer syne thou arte slayne wythout deser te thrugh foule horryble dethe wherfor dere sone bodily feliship twyned must nede departed fro soo shall berye whyder shall thy moost soroufull moder goo shall duelle dere sone hou maye lyue wythout sothly wolde gladly beryed wyth soo yt soo euer thou myght wyth sythen maye beryed wyth bodily att leest shall beryed ghostly mynde wherfore shal berye thi body thy graue soule therfore comende leue swete sone hou soroufull departynge discyples whiche lower degree thanne apostle done proude men woll gladly goo speke conuersaute wyth hem ben grete fame hyghe astate towarde world yet ferd er shewed mekenesse thyrde poynt ayenst samarytane ouer maye consyder grete godenes lorde jhu processe gospel sayd saye enformeth disciple maneres also fedeth comforteth specyally feynyth hym goo ferder vnto ende kyndle encreace desyre affeccon hym feruently bydden witholden hem ferdermore beningnely entreth goth hem takith brede blessith wyth holy hondes brekyth yeuyth hem thene shewyth hymself hem thus dooth wyth v euery day ghostly wolde bydde v dwell wyth v drawen wyth feruent desire deuoute prayer holy dytacons therfor hath taught v behouyth euer praye fayle take mynde werkes pyte hospitalyte suffyceth rede ye wordes biddynges god ben performed dede may playnly enformed omely saynt gregory vpon gospell last lorde ihus willynge also wisyte comforte dwelled longe wyth thise discyples assone broken yeuen hem brede vanysshed awaye fro eyen p lorde ihus appered apostle discyples yt reclused drede self daye resurreccon caplm lvii whan two forsaid dyscyples thus comforted sayde presence oure lorde anone joye tourned agayne jherusalem camen appostles discyples pryuely gadred thomas absent told hem forsaid processe herden agayn warde theymthat soothly lorde rysen hath appered peter wyth sodeynly oure lorde jhesus entryn ge hem yates closed stode middes hem sayd pee anone fallynge doune erth cetera lrnowlegynge gylte soo lefte hym forsaken receyueden hym wyth grete joye thenne sayd hem ryseth vp bretherne goode coforte al synes ben foryeue soo stondeth thus amonge discyples spekyng homely wyth hem shewynge hem booth honde syde openyth wyttes vnderstondynge cleerly holy scryptures knowe sothfastly resurreccon asketh whether haue oughte eten etith homely hem part rosted fysshe hony combe preue body present rysen bretheth hem yeuith h holy ghost loo yf take juwardly hede thise forsa de thynges ben full swete full ghostly lykynge thenne disciple joyefull syghte lorde whiche dredfull heuy lorde god gladly yeuen hym askyth truely serued mynystred hym merily stoden aboute hym herwyth beholde lady blessed moder present tyme discyples gad ed takyth hede al thynges done swete sone wyth vnspekable joye sittynge hym homly seruinge hym full gladly lorde takyth gladly seruyce worshippeth therwyth discyples yet morouer foryete mary maudleyne byloued discyplesse thapostles apostlesse olde manere sittyth fete mayster besily hereth wordes may gladly gode wyll minystreth lorde jhu worthy reason shall fully brenne leuynge goo gloryous ascencon p ascencon lorde jhesu caplm lxii touchynge wonderfull ascencyon oure lorde jhesu thou herest redest yf thou wolt fele swetnes therof woll thou wakeli quicke thi soule ferforth yf euer herby fore byden yu madest deuoute yma gynacon present hys wordes dedes yu doo moche wyth alle thy myght solempne nyte passeth shall clerly shewe wyth forth processe namly one thing shold stire herte thyn entencon quyck thin affeccon yt thy lord passyng away fro bodily presece tyme pylgrymage erth fully coplete ended wherfore wordes dedes may attetyfly discyples whiche shall pryncipally foude destroye true fayth blessed sacrament grete clergy mane cunynge merueyles myracles werchynge saynt gregory morale vpon worde cryst gospel spekynge antecryst discyples sayth sentence shall ryse vp fals crysten men fals prophetes shal shew werke grete sygnes wonder somoche ben goddis chosen folke yf maye shall brought errour sothly sayth saynt gregory oure true marterswerchen merueylles tyme suffren tormentes paynes thene saye comyng antcryst discyples whan yeuen tormentes paynes shal also therwith werche miracle lete v thenne thinke haue mynde temptacyons mannes thought shall whanne meke marter submyttith body tormentes neuertheles tormentour eyen werchyth myracles whoos vertue shall thene soo sadly grounded byseue ne shall meued thoughte tyme seeth tormenteth also therwyth sygnes merueylles openly shyneth thene shal antecryst highe worship merueilous werchyng harde sharpe cruelte tormentyng thise ben wordes holy doctour saint gregori many moo spekynges wond er full myghte antcryst discyples grete temptacon shall tyme crysten men lykely reason mooste cofort cristen byleue stant moost excellent sacrament crystes body soo antcryst discyples shall princypally werke destruccon fyrst tru bylene blessed sacrament forsayd two maners say clergye euydence worldes cunyng acordyng naturell reason many merueyles myracles werchyng false decepcon fyrste maner werchyng haue seen dayes discyples antecryst ben called lollardes haue made moche descencyon diuysion holy chirche put mani men errour blessed sacramet fals doctryne mayster whiche thrugh grete clergye cunynge phylosophye deceyued yaue cred ce doctryne arystotle stant onely naturell reyson man thanne dyde doctryne holy chyrche true doctours therof touchynge precyous sacrament arystotle techyth kyndely reason accordeth accydentes brede wyne say colour sauour soo forth may substauce brede wyne kynde doctryne holy chirche blessed sacrament specyal myracle god aboue kynde colour sauonr accydentes brede wyne ben wythout kyndly sub ecte say without substauce brede wine consecracon asmoche doctryne holy chirche ayest prynciples philosophye naturell scyence therfore mayster lollardes reproued scorned errith made many erre touchyng bileue holiest sacrament whiche yeuen credence hym opinyon grete clergye true doctryne holy chyrche thus yet dayes hath antcryst wrought fyrst maner befor sayd fals mayster lollardes many discyples destruccon true cristen byleue touchyng blessed sacrament cristis body many poyntes ayenste holy chirche wythout seconde maner say werchynge merueylles myracles antecriste hem soo grete power wyth reason also wroughte merueylles myracles lykely holy chirche true byleue specially blessed sacrament grete party destroyed vnstablenes moost party peple notwithstondyng grete merueyles myracles many ofte lorde hath shewed herbefore holy sacrament sayd strength v stable v true byleue holy chirche hath taught v whiche byleue reason shold soo sadly sentence apostle poul though came doun angel heuen taughte contrary sholde yeue credence hym holde hym cursed sooth maye noo true angel teche contrary bileue holy chirche therfor soo dooth angell sathanas god ben fals lollardes whiche haue neyther true drede perfyte loue oure lord jhu therfore fele ghostly swetnes heuenly mete precyous body ne likynge mynde merueylles shewed blessed sacramente thorugh grace stonden true byleue holy chyrche hath taught v souerayne holyest sacrament wyth goostly lykynge sowle haue oonly mynde grete merueylles myghty myracles wryten preched holy sacrament dyuerse maners shewed beforsayd also consider lorde jhus vnspeable goodnes shewed mankynde yeueth hym self v euery daye bodily precious sacrament conclusion moost specyall mynde blessed lyf souerayne comforte helpe wretchid lyfe whyche full temptacons ouersette wyth many enmyes wherfore spedfull v contynuelly crye helpe sonerayne vertue blessed sacrament wordes holy chyrche syngeth ympne sacrament thus thou helful oost openest door heue bataylles enmyes oppressen ouerseten v wherfore yeue v strengthe wythstondynge brynge v thy helpe ouercomyng also wythstondynge temptacons ouercomyng vice getynge vertues encreace feruent affeccons lorde jhu full ende blessed lyfe wryten p enprynted wynkin worth p folowyth shorte deuoute prayer jhu cryst body sacrament aulter whiche oweth sayd presence holy sacrament masse inwarde deuocon heyle holyest body lorde jhesu cryste art soothfastly conteyned moost excellent sacrament knowlege lorde god wyth mouth loue wyth herte desyre wyth inwarde affeccyon soule beseche swete jhu thou vochesauf thy souerayne goodnes daye soo benygnely gracyously vysite sike soule desiryng receyue goostly heelfull sacrifyce well grace soo may wyth gladnesse fynde medecyne heele body soule vertue thy blessed presence beholde lorde jhu wickydnesse manyfolde neclygences grete vnkyndnes rather thy souerayne mercy endles godenes sothly thou arte holy lambe wythout weme syne yt day offred euerlastinge fader heuen redempcon al ye worlde thou swettest mana angel mete thou moost likynge ghostly drynke brynge inwarde mouth hony swete taast thy helfull presence byadie feruour thy charyte quenche maner vyces shede plentee vertues encreace ye yeftes grace yeue heele body soule thy plesynge god biseche thou wolt soo gracyously bowe fro thy hye heuen come doune knytted joyned made one spiryte wyth worshypfull sacrament byseche al myn enmyes put awaye fro strengthe synnes foryeue wyckidnes excluded blessid presence good purpose lorde yeue thou maners thou correcte amende al werkes dedes thou dispose thy wyll wytte vnd er stondyng swete jhu made clere wyth newe lyghte grace myne affeccon enflamed wyth fyre thy loue myne hope coforted strengthed wyth blessid sacrament soo lyf profyte euer amendynge better last fro wretchid worlde wyth blessed departyng maye come wyth lyf euerlastyng jhu lorde vertue grace thy lyfe blessed wythout endynge amen amen amen p jhu lorde thy blessid lyfe helpe comforte wretchid lyfe amen p explicit speclm vite xpi cu tili ime tractatu breue de sacramento corporis xpi oracone eid sacramenti impressu
